    ฿฿฿฿฿  ฿฿฿฿฿   ฿             ฿฿฿ฐ฿฿ฐ     ฿
                ฿฿฿฿        ฿  e d i t o r i a l !  ฿

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear RCN,                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Well, I have just finished reading most of RCN #17, I especially      บ
 บ  liked how only one side of the story was presented about the #ROR         บ
 บ  takeover by Razor 1911.  In a minute, I will explain how everything got   บ
 บ  started, but first, I would like to comment on whoever did the interview  บ
 บ  for RCN.                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      RCN editors have recently been talking a lot of the use of the word   บ
 บ  lame to describe, saying it is over used and that most of the people      บ
 บ  saying it are the lame ones.  The person who conducted the interview for  บ
 บ  RCN, flat out call ROR lame.  I am not sure who was doing this            บ
 บ  interview, but I would assume it was Rebel Chicken.  If I remember        บ
 บ  you've run 3 basic shit groups, and you have the balls to call another    บ
 บ  group lame?                                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      In ROR's worst time, it kicked the fuck out of VND or FSW.  An        บ
 บ  unbiased emag?  I don't think so.  I was on the Internet the entire time  บ
 บ  the shit went down, NEVER ONCE, was I asked for ROR's side of the story.  บ
 บ  If you had time to get Razor 1911's side, you had time to get ROR's.  Or  บ
 บ  maybe you're too "lame" to do that much at one time?                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Now, onto how this all unfolded.  ROR has had many problems with      บ
 บ  takeover, usually because of friends.  We op someone on a friends list,   บ
 บ  then they op someone else.  This was the case that night.  Rom Racer, as  บ
 บ  he often does, had ops in #ROR.  A ROR member named KH was in the         บ
 บ  channel, Rom Racer banned KH, after being told a few times before over    บ
 บ  the past 2 days, not to ban or kick members.  After KH was re-added to    บ
 บ  the bot (user lists had been reset), he ban kicked Rom Racer.  Other      บ
 บ  Razor 1911 members who had ops started trying to do mass deops, one of    บ
 บ  these people included Loloc, and ROR member when I saw people starting    บ
 บ  to do mass deops, I started to ban kick them to get things under          บ
 บ  control, during all of the deopping and kicking the channel became        บ
 บ  desynched.                                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      While doing a resynch, I became heavily lagged, and Loloc managed to  บ
 บ  get into #ROR, and get ops, he opped several Razor members who tookover   บ
 บ  the channel.  After talking to a few Razor 1911 people, we were able to   บ
 บ  get things under control, and worked out, and soon got #ROR back.  End    บ
 บ  of story.                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Manic                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear Manic,                                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Razor 1911 came up to me and asked for an interview.  I searched for  บ
 บ  ROR members but could not find any.  You've just presented your side of   บ
 บ  the story, and I consider that a rebuttal.  End of story.                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  *PS* You failed to mention how ROR was trying to take over #Razor.        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Hitex/Rebel Chicken       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear RCN,                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Alright, so we saw at least 3-5 couriering groups come and go last    บ
 บ  year. at least 10 release groups, and I dont say games or utils, since    บ
 บ  all the groups that were formed in 1995-1996 besides.. err CORP.. and     บ
 บ  umm Legacy, are going in both directions which is completely lame.        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      So now we have a scene, where every guy who has a shell and phoenix   บ
 บ  and who is not banned from #exceed, considers himself a part of.  A       บ
 บ  scene  proud of having 40 releases a day,  35 of which, I can say right   บ
 บ  now, will not work.  Come to think of it , most of what will seem to      บ
 บ  work, will be shareware, or will not be 100% cracked.                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      There are exactly 5 groups on the scene that I trust enough, to be    บ
 บ  downloading their releases, and knowing they will work.  As sad as it     บ
 บ  may sound it is the truth.  I will tell an even sadder example, a lame    บ
 บ  group , releases a lame ware that might actually work that I might want   บ
 บ  for one reason or another.  The lame group then gives the release to a    บ
 บ  lame "official" couriering group and what do we get?  Elite couriers,     บ
 บ  fresh off #warez950, trading the release in ascii mode.  I fucking swear  บ
 บ  I have seen more than one example of that.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Why do release groups rate every ware they release as a 10/10 ware?   บ
 บ  I understand its cool to have a good util and rate it high, but when a    บ
 บ  group like, lets not mention names here, releases a ware "Pastry Mixer    บ
 บ  for windows 95 xx/50" where all the content was ripped and only the       บ
 บ  coolest .wavs and .avis were left within the release; goes and states,    บ
 บ  ok 10/10 for this one.  Give me a fucking break..  the group just earns   บ
 บ  itself a shitty reputation, and after a few releases like that, it is     บ
 บ  banned from all major boards and sites (all the releases from xxx group   บ
 บ  are nuked automatically, regardless of content).                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I still haven't given credit where its due.  As shitty as everything  บ
 บ  may seem, we still have excellent groups, releasing quality warez, to     บ
 บ  keep the scene going.  We still see good boards, have 0 hour files, the   บ
 บ  way it should be.  We still have the good sites, getting gigs of 0 min    บ
 บ  stuff weekly.  What can I say?  It's all up to the people we will hand    บ
 บ  the scene over to in a few years, to decide whether they want to make it  บ
 บ  worse, or better, or destroy it completely (damn, you never know what     บ
 บ  those #Warez950 people are capable of).                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Well, that's it for my little $0.02, have fun, trade lots, and get    บ
 บ  good grades in school.  Grades are very, very important (those of you     บ
 บ  who are still in kindergarten, please disregard that message).            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Arch Vile (DOD/PSG/RiSC)  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      You're absolutely right, the funny thing is, the #Exceed leeches are  บ
 บ  the future of the scene.                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Hitex/Rebel Chicken       บ

 บ  Dear RCN,                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hi!  This is Miller.  I couldn't help but notice how much bull shit   บ
 บ  is said about fATE.  Just because you are somebody else doesn't mean      บ
 บ  they're slow, they suck, or any other bull shit comments.  I myself am a  บ
 บ  fATE head, and I seriously think you should try to avoid group bashing,   บ
 บ  especially if it's a group that HAS been in the scene for over a year.    บ
 บ  And if you're gonna talk shit about groups, then talk shit about some     บ
 บ  lamer group, and DON'T TELL ME TO CALM DOWN!!  I'VE HAD ENOUGH OF THIS    บ
 บ  BULL SHIT!                                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Miller                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear Miller,                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Alright, this is a response not just to Miller but to everybody that  บ
 บ  thinks similarly about anything that was ever posted about RCN.  Before   บ
 บ  you make such a harsh accusation of somebody, check yourself first.  I    บ
 บ  don't mean to make a public humiliation out of Miller, but I would be     บ
 บ  very impressed if you could just ONCE point out any place where any RCN   บ
 บ  Editor (Rebel Chicken or Hitex) has ever group bashed on fATE.  Alright,  บ
 บ  I've given you plenty of time to think, so now that you know you're       บ
 บ  wrong (yes, apology accepted) let's explain a little about what it means  บ
 บ  to accuse RCN of such a task.                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      When someone submits an article or an interview, it is HIS/HER        บ
 บ  opinion only.  Do I need to make a fuckin' disclaimer?  I don't think     บ
 บ  so.  That's lame.  This is an e-mag and everybody in the scene should     บ
 บ  have enough goddamned common sense to figure out that if it doesn't say   บ
 บ  the name of any RCN editor at the top, it's not necessarily the view of   บ
 บ  RCN as a whole!  In fact, if it does say the name of an RCN Editor, it's  บ
 บ  not necessarily that of an RCN writer.  What is RCN?  No, not the e-mag   บ
 บ  part.  What makes up the RCN Backbone?  It's the editors and the          บ
 บ  coordinators (such as RoadRebel).                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      If you're a writer but you don't write for a week, your name will     บ
 บ  not be in the credits that week.  If you're an editor, however, you are   บ
 บ  responsible for what you say and it is assumed that your feelings are     บ
 บ  also that of any other editor.  If you ever see Hitex or Rebel Chicken    บ
 บ  bash any group, you will then be able to say we group bashed, but until   บ
 บ  then, it is simply the views of someone that wrote for RCN.               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      If the Chairman of Microsoft were to write for PC Magazine bashing    บ
 บ  IBM, I would assume none of you would go out and accuse PC Magazine of    บ
 บ  bashing IBM.  The same respect should be extended to RCN.                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  The RCN Staff             บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear RCN,                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      So many people trade warez today.  So many people striving to be the  บ
 บ  best they can be and having the highest "position" in the scene.  So      บ
 บ  many people staying up for hours on end to courier that new release,      บ
 บ  crack that new game, make their group the best.  Do these people have     บ
 บ  ANY lives?  Don't get me wrong I LOVE warez and the scene and it takes    บ
 บ  up A LOT of my time, but it's fun and that's what we are all here for.    บ
 บ  The reason trading warez is so enjoyable is because the warez world is    บ
 บ  an imaginary one, we rule it.  WE have the high positions.  WE are        บ
 บ  considered to be GODS.  This is very cool because in the real world       บ
 บ  (most of us) are students and kids.  Constatly being told "No, you can't  บ
 บ  do this; No, you can't do that." The warez world lets us escape into a    บ
 บ  fantasy world, a world of our own.                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The only problem with this is when the fantasy warez world starts to  บ
 บ  rule our "real world".  People who stay on the net for days on end with   บ
 บ  no sleep and only stopping to eat and piss.  I have been a victim of      บ
 บ  this many times before and I want it to STOP.  The world of warez does    บ
 บ  not have any effect on the real world whatsoever.  Don't get me wrong I   บ
 บ  LOVE the scene and warez, but there is a point where it has to stop.      บ
 บ  Trading warez is VERY fun and that is the number one reason people do     บ
 บ  it.  The competition is also a very big reason.  Competing through warez  บ
 บ  is like any sport you can think of.  A bunch of teams (Groups) compete    บ
 บ  against one another and try to score points (Release/Crack/Whatever your  บ
 บ  speciality is in the Scene). Doing this gives us all a rush and makes us  บ
 บ  feel special.  I don't want to sound dumb, but you can't deny it.  When   บ
 บ  someone releases an awesome ware that everyone wants to download they     บ
 บ  feel like "the shit".  I guess this is enough reason to be in the scene   บ
 บ  because it is fun, it is enjoyable.                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Those who criticize us usually don't have an understanding about how  บ
 บ  fun it is.  Well, think about it, how much fun does it sound to sit on    บ
 บ  the computer for hours and type away at whatever your doing.  I guess     บ
 บ  it's worth it but that's my opinion, yours might be different.            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I have one more thing to say.  Groups who fight all the time and      บ
 บ  hate eachother are stupid.  The scene was created to have competition     บ
 บ  and fun, not to hate others who are trying to do the same thing you are.  บ
 บ  Everyone is here to do what they do best, specializing in one field or    บ
 บ  another. Ask yourself, if you are criticizing someone else, what makes    บ
 บ  me so much better than them.  We are all here for the same purpose,       บ
 บ  don't spoil it for everyone.                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Bollox                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ

 บ  Dear RCN,                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Starting as of June 16, 1996, #warez+ is back in busines.  They       บ
 บ  decided to have a bit of a reunion, so they reopened the channel.  The    บ
 บ  original ops are back also.  Channel Warez+ was always one of the best    บ
 บ  WarezX channels.  Although now when people join the channel, no one even  บ
 บ  remembers it and say thing like, "Oh great, another lame warez channel".  บ
 บ  Warez+ was always the hangout of the more elite warez "traders".  Right   บ
 บ  now it is just anyone and everyone + their dog. They are currently        บ
 บ  trying to get off the ground again, and once again striving to become an  บ
 บ  elite warezX trading channel.  As far as I have seen, they are doing a    บ
 บ  good job.  The ops are very nice, not the typical "I dont like that, so   บ
 บ  I will kick-ban you" ops.                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Although, I do have one small complaint, which is the auto kick-ban   บ
 บ  of *!*@*.ipt.aol.com, because I dont think it is fair to be prejudiced    บ
 บ  and say that all users from AOL are not worthy enough to be in a warezX   บ
 บ  trading channel, because I know of some very elite people from AOL, that  บ
 บ  have the online service for other reasons then "its so easy and friendly  บ
 บ  to use".                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Other then that, I like #warez+, and believe it should be supported   บ
 บ  by anyone and everyone. My suggestion to the ops is to get some Offer     บ
 บ  Bots going in there, just to make it pick up users, and maybe try some    บ
 บ  things that other channels haven't.                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      And another thing, I know that you are barely restarting the          บ
 บ  channel, and not too many people know about it, but anything you do       บ
 บ  DON'T MASS INVITE!  Advertise it to your friends and have them join,      บ
 บ  then let them personally tell people to join. Not just so you wont annoy  บ
 บ  people, but the probability is that these users will be dedicated to      บ
 บ  your channel rather then #warez5, #warez950, #warez666, and such. Think   บ
 บ  if you would like somebody mass inviting in you channel for               บ
 บ  #warez<whatever>. I dont think you would, so dont do it.                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Back on the subject of banning ISP's, I have been getting more and    บ
 บ  more pissed off lately. I am a Netcom Dial-Up PPP/SLIP user. Not only am  บ
 บ  I K-Lined from every EFNet server, but now I am banned from a majority    บ
 บ  of Warez Channels. I hang out on WarezX channels about 1% or less of my   บ
 บ  time that I am on iRC, so this really doesnt affect me. But there are A   บ
 บ  LOT of traders that can bring in a lot of warez and trades for your       บ
 บ  channel, but you have ALL Netcom users banned on your bots. If you feel   บ
 บ  guilty (which you should), please take the *!*@*.ix.netcom.com ban off    บ
 บ  of your bots.  Thank You and Goodnight.                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Kang                      บ

 บ  like that need to get out of the way of the bigger groups and let the     บ
 บ  experienced people handle the scene, or get their shit together and       บ
 บ  start doing things properly, the right way.  I know it's not easy, I      บ
 บ  mean god, I couldn't run a decent release group, let alone be a           บ
 บ  dedicated courier, but if you are going to spend your time (and that of   บ
 บ  others) releasing shit, you best do it right.                             บ

 บ  Dear RCN,                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      It seems like today a lot of the people affiliated with the scene     บ
 บ  have begun to designate everyone as either a lamer or an elite.  Almost   บ
 บ  everyone on IRC yells "LAMER" at someone else because of something as     บ
 บ  simple as a file request.  Similarly, if someone belongs to a group, be   บ
 บ  him the lowliest courier who doesn't even do half his share, in many      บ
 บ  channels will be revealed as elite.  This 'elite' designation also falls  บ
 บ  on channel ops, who often get op status for nothing other than IRC        บ
 บ  relation to the other ops.                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I've been around the warez scene for at least 12 years.  I can        บ
 บ  remember when couriering really ment COURIERING.  300 bps modems          บ
 บ  couldn't compare with walking to a friend's house with a handful of       บ
 บ  5.25" disks and just copying what new stuff he had.  I'll bet hardly      บ
 บ  anyone in the scene today can name members of groups like Eaglesoft, DCS  บ
 บ  (Doughnut Cracking Service), and a few others.                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      But does knowing these things make me elite?  I hope that that fact   บ
 บ  alone does NOT.  I've pretty much done it all, opped warez channels, run  บ
 บ  a BBS, and done freelance couriering between FTP sites and BBSs.  I even  บ
 บ  coded some BBS mods.  Still, I was never part of an official group.  So   บ
 บ  am I a lamer because I never had my name at the bottom of a grop .NFO     บ
 บ  file?  I hope not.  The point is this - warez, in its entirety, is a      บ
 บ  win-win situation for practically everyone in the scene.  Why someone     บ
 บ  who enters a channel asking for a particular ware gets branded a lamer    บ
 บ  and kicked, while 3 idlers sit motionless watching the world go by, is a  บ
 บ  mystery to me.  The only 'lamers' in the warez scene are those who work   บ
 บ  to destroy it.                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Wildgoose                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  *PS* Keep up the good work!  The mag continues to be the only emag        บ
 บ  (warez or otherwise) that I read on a regular basis.                      บ

 บ  Dear RCN,                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I was shocked when I read RCN #17 this past weekend.  After reading   บ
 บ  your interview with Endeavour, founder of COPS, and making my own         บ
 บ  assessment of COPS, I wondered if anything could possibly be in a sadder  บ
 บ  shape than COPS.                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      COPS' NFO is one of the worst ones I've EVER seen.  Whoever drew it   บ
 บ  lacks talent and the person that added the text should be charged with    บ
 บ  plagiarism.  These guys lack originality and most of their information    บ
 บ  comes from other groups.  They have ripped off parts of DOD, Razor, and   บ
 บ  PWA's NFOs.  The only original statement is the group's quote and that    บ
 บ  is one of hypocrisy.  "COPS will beat you and you will like it!"  The     บ
 บ  only thing these poor bastards will be beating is their meat.             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Endeavour, if the indication that you guys coming on strong is        บ
 บ  through your releases, may God help you all.  When a non-foreign group    บ
 บ  starts releasing software in another language, then you know it is in     บ
 บ  trouble.  A few weeks ago, COPS released MS-Access in Chinese.  What is   บ
 บ  wrong with you people? Less than 15% of the scene is Asian or even        บ
 บ  Chinese and I'm pretty sure the majority of these people is content with  บ
 บ  their English versions.  There is nothing like preparing an English       บ
 บ  database in a Chinese program.  Also, when you released Blake Stone, you  บ
 บ  knew that the files dated back to 1993, yet you gave the go-ahead to      บ
 บ  release.  This indicates your sloppy leadership and the sad shape that    บ
 บ  COPS is in.  For no decent group leader, including groups smaller than    บ
 บ  yours, would have released such crap that one can find in the bargain     บ
 บ  bin at your local software store.  At the rate you guys are coming on     บ
 บ  strong, it may take COPS a century to reach the magnitute of what         บ
 บ  Mortality is today.                                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Endeavour, you have no right to rag on Malice.  I remember back in    บ
 บ  February, you used to come into #MALiCE and beg us to courier your        บ
 บ  releases.  We kicked and kicked yet you kept on rejoining the channel.    บ
 บ  I have to admit, you are very persistent and arrogant.  Otherwise, COPS   บ
 บ  would not be alive today.  You think that Malice is dead today, but       บ
 บ  they'll always have more of a fighting chance to regroup than COPS.  I    บ
 บ  am surprised that fATE accepted COPS under their protective wing.         บ
 บ  Surely, fATE has more sense and respectability than that.  But then       บ
 บ  again, fATE is a second-rate couriering group.  Any decent courier group  บ
 บ  will not have a releasing division to back up and/or supplement their     บ
 บ  couriering.  I hope that Doobie will come to his senses and kick you out  บ
 บ  as Malice has done.                                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      In conclusion, the only thing COPS will "professionally" specialize   บ
 บ  in is crap.  In fact, why not change the name to Crappy Old Pirated       บ
 บ  Shareware? This name would state the true nature of COPS.  If you guys    บ
 บ  are coming on strong, then groups such as PWA must be flying in a         บ
 บ  rocket.  If a member of COPS today is the NEW batch and holds the key to  บ
 บ  the future of the scene, then perhaps we should all quit or retire now    บ
 บ  to avoid the pain and humiliation that will come later.                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  kT!                       บ

 บ  Dear RCN,                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I'm just writing out of disgust.  My story is a common one, but       บ
 บ  nevertheless, a sad one.  I used to be a lamer <CRINGE!> just like        บ
 บ  everyone else (I find it extremely hard to believe that any of you        บ
 บ  started out by moving files for RiSC!).  But, like one dude said in RCN   บ
 บ  #17 (there's no skill in warez, just contacts), I had made some good      บ
 บ  contacts and I moved up the warez 'pyramid.'  It was a long climb, and I  บ
 บ  came nowhere near the top, but I don't give two shits about that now!  I  บ
 บ  was involved in the fledgling community several years ago, and my         บ
 บ  involvement has carrived to today.  I have several past and present       บ
 บ  affiliations, but nothing like RiSC or Prestige.  You see, a long time    บ
 บ  ago in the world of warez, I realized that those on the top were          บ
 บ  dropping like flies, and although they had worked long and hard to get    บ
 บ  there, they were all burnt out!  I was and still am a 0-6 MONTH trader,   บ
 บ  and you know what?  It doesn't matter!  It doens't fucking matter at      บ
 บ  all!  I have seen the 'elite' come and go, and it never changes.  Sure,   บ
 บ  I think it would be cool someday to have 5 phone lines all dedicated to   บ
 บ  moving files, but is it worth giving up my life for?  No, not at all!     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      You see, people in 'the scene' are always saying stuff like 'Man,     บ
 บ  you gotta take responsibility for your actions, you gotta relize that     บ
 บ  you could be arrested,' but ironically, these same people don't take      บ
 บ  responsibility for their involvement.  I know people are flying through   บ
 บ  the ranks of warez faster than ever now, but what happens?  They all end  บ
 บ  up on the far end of the spectrum, under the 'burnt out' category.        บ
 บ  People don't seem to realize what's going on.  If you're going to take    บ
 บ  responsibility for trading commercial software illegally, you have to     บ
 บ  take responsibility for your rise in doing so.  It pisses me off to hear  บ
 บ  people complain about how they have no life because of warez, and that    บ
 บ  warez ruined them, and that they become burnt out and retire.  I realize  บ
 บ  for some people, myself included, being involved for a long period of     บ
 บ  time does take its toll, and I feel that if you have spent the past 4-or  บ
 บ  so, or however many years moving files, that you deserve the retirement   บ
 บ  you take, but these people that fly through in a matter of weeks, or      บ
 บ  even months, I mean get real people!                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      It's all about responsibility and maturity.  Take it slow, there's    บ
 บ  no big deal about it.  It's a hobby, and hobbies are supposed to be fun,  บ
 บ  right?  I hope this will serve as a rude awakening for some of you.  If   บ
 บ  you're just starting out, don't feel intimidated by the bigger, older     บ
 บ  elite members of the community.  Don't feel pressured into spending 16    บ
 บ  hours of YOUR day behind a computer pressing buttons and moving 0         บ
 บ  nanosecond warez.  For me, warez is just a hobby, and I don't plan on     บ
 บ  changing anything.  I am perfectly satisfied doing this in my free time.  บ
 บ  If that makes me 'less-l337' than you, so what?  I only do this in the    บ
 บ  evening and when I have or need some time to relax for a bit.             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I guarantee to you it will be more fun for me and I will be around    บ
 บ  longer. If you're already established in the scene, maybe this will help  บ
 บ  you re-evaluate what you're doing.  I don't think warez is bad at all,    บ
 บ  but I think all those involved need to take more responsibility for the   บ
 บ  scene.  When it gets to the point where it is no longer fun, i is         บ
 บ  tedious and a job and you feel pressured into doing it, take a break!     บ
 บ  Even if that means cutting back from 15+ megs a day to 75+ and then 50+,  บ
 บ  do yourself a favor, and do everyone else involved a favor.  Be           บ
 บ  responsible.  If you're going to get involved, fine, just don't bail out  บ
 บ  in 6 months' time and say you are all burnt out and you have no life and  บ
 บ  just bitch and complain about the scene.  Consider yourself warned.       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Zero Lucifer              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Reporter : Hitex                     Interviewee : Ustasa               บ
 บ    Subject  : RiSC Loses to Everlast    Affiliation : Everlast Member      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Can you give me a rough picture of who you are and how you pertain  บ
 บ        to the warez scene?                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  EVR : I'm basically just a courier that can be very dedicated to the      บ
 บ        scene.  I know everyone knows just how much I love the scene!  I    บ
 บ        started out 4 years ago and very slowly worked my way up.  It       บ
 บ        takes much loyalty and dedication to get places.                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What are some of your prior affiliations?                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  EVR : I've been a part of RiSC, Razor 1911, Tyranny, Genesis,             บ
 บ        Generation-X, Everlast, Prophecy, Scum, Pirates with Attitudes,     บ
 บ        Drink or Die, Hybrid, Dynamix, and few others not worth             บ
 บ        mentioning.                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Which of these affiliations did you most treasure and enjoy being   บ
 บ        a part of?                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  EVR : To tell you the truth, RiSC, but as you might know, I left for      บ
 บ        some undisputed reasons.  RiSC is the best group ever.  Very loyal  บ
 บ        people like Eagle 1, Enforcer, Pharaoh, and Crackpot, make RiSC     บ
 บ        what it is.  I was treated with respect in the group.               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What were the reasons for your departure from RiSC?                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  EVR : I had an argument with a netmonkey by the name of Suspicious        บ
 บ        Image.  He thought he could boss me around in the group, so I said  บ
 บ        screw this shit and left!  For example, he would threaten to get    บ
 บ        me kicked out due to inactivity and so on, so I said to myself who  บ
 บ        the fuck does this lamer think he is!?                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : So you went and joined Everlast?  Would that have been a second     บ
 บ        choice to RiSC?  Which do you enjoy more?                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  EVR : Well, I joined Everlast so I couldn't really tell you who is        บ
 บ        better to me, but Everlast is a bunch of good friends that joined   บ
 บ        together to make the group.  It's really cool.  Mr. Skill,          บ
 บ        Asmodeus, Blue Adept, Shatter Star, Immortal, are all pretty cool   บ
 บ        guys.                                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : I seem to remember that Shatter Star was in RiSC for a short        บ
 บ        while.  Yet he, too, left for Everlast.  Could this be said to be   บ
 บ        an overall statement about the attitudes of RiSC versus those of    บ
 บ        Everlast?                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  EVR : Yes.  To tell you the truth, I'm not the only one that left         บ
 บ        because of Sispicious Image.  There are others.  People like him    บ
 บ        seem to make the group lame, and I think action should be taken     บ
 บ        towards people like him.  To tell you the truth, I think RiSC is    บ
 บ        falling apart.                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : RiSC, in your opinion, is falling apart.  Do you mean, in other     บ
 บ        words, that Everlast is taking RiSC's old place in the scene?       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  EVR : No, I think RiSC will always be a dominant group, but it'll just    บ
 บ        lose its touch.  Everlast kicks ass, but I can't tell you the       บ
 บ        future man.                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What do you think of a "new" (revamped) group called GODS?  They    บ
 บ        have split up both Digital and Amnesia to form themselves, what do  บ
 บ        you expect this will do to the couriering scene?                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  EVR : To tell ya the truth, I think this GODS group will kick some ass,   บ
 บ        but we'll just have to see how long they'll last.  Groups come and  บ
 บ        go these days.  Kinda reminds me of my old group Cartel.  They      บ
 บ        seem to have some pretty cool guys in there, but they will have to  บ
 บ        establish themeselves on the big boards like Akira and Park         บ
 บ        Central.  RiSC and Everlast are kicking ass on the boards.          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Does Everlast have any organized IRC channels going for it yet?     บ

 บ    Reporter : Lucifers Fear             Interviewee : Demaxxus             บ
 บ    Subject  : Demaxxus Returns          Affiliation : n/a                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : You were recently busted and raided by the RCMP (Royal Canadia      บ
 บ        Mounted Police), but now I hear that you are back in the scene.     บ
 บ        Is that true, and if so, how are you able to come back to the       บ
 บ        scene?                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DEM : Well, the police didn't have enough evidence on me so they had to   บ
 บ        give me back my computer hardware that they confiscated.  The main  บ
 บ        charges were for stolen merchandise, but when the confiscated       บ
 บ        hardware was not the stolen material they were looking for, they    บ
 บ        were forced to give my stuff back and let me go.  They basically    บ
 บ        had dick-all for evidence.  Although they said they were going to   บ
 บ        be keeping an eye on me, which probably means having a fat cop      บ
 บ        watching me all day to see if I go into any computer stores, that   บ
 บ        fat cop will probably be too busy eating donuts to catch me.        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : How did the RCMP found out that you were Demaxxus in the first      บ
 บ        place?                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DEM : I honestly have no idea how they found me.  The only way I can      บ
 บ        think of is if one of the stores I've "found" stuff from gave the   บ
 บ        police my name.  I was recently caught on video tape at Future      บ
 บ        Shop getting a modem, so they would have had a picture of me to     บ
 บ        give to the police.  Either that, or one of the RATS from our area  บ
 บ        code (most famously known for ratting on Anarchist) made a little   บ
 บ        anonymous phone call.                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Is it true that they actually tapped your phone line to get         บ
 บ        evidence, and if so, how long did they listen in on your            บ
 บ        interesting phonecalls?                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DEM : Well, I'm not sure if they actually tapped my line, in fact, in     บ
 บ        this technologically impaired city, I highly doubt it.  Although    บ
 บ        they must have been checking on my phone line somehow, because      บ
 บ        when they first came to my house, they briefly spoke about          บ
 บ        carding, but that was it, they never mentioned it after that.       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What did you think when the RCMP was at your door 7:30 a.m. with a  บ
 บ        warrant?                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DEM : My first thought was, "Fuck, what did my brother do now", but when  บ
 บ        they asked for me, I almost shit a brick.  I couldn't believe       บ
 บ        they'd finally caught up to me.  I thought that they might have     บ
 บ        come to my house because I used to be on Anarchist's board, but     บ
 บ        then they told me they were at my house with a warrant in regard    บ
 บ        to stolen merchandise.                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : We all love our famous RCMP officer by the name of TOM JAMES, but   บ
 บ        would he have been the one leading this investigation that led to   บ
 บ        your bust?                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DEM : No, to my surprise, he never entered this situation at all.  I      บ
 บ        don't even think it was the RCMP (RCMP = Royal Canadian Mounted     บ
 บ        Police = Canadian FBI), it was just the local police.  I was kind   บ
 บ        of sad when he didn't show up, I didn't have a chance to give him   บ
 บ        a mint and a bottle of scope.  I guess he wasn't part of my bust    บ
 บ        because the warrant for my bust had nothing to do with the          บ
 บ        Anarchist, and the topic was just on stolen property.  Neither the  บ
 บ        RCMP nor Tom James was in on my bust.                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : I was informed that you weren't happy about something which was     บ
 บ        making a front page in the newspaper, is this true and how come a   บ
 บ        local story like this not make it?                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DEM : YES!  I was fucking pissed off when they didn't have my bust in     บ
 บ        the newspaper, nevermind the front page.  If (when) I get busted,   บ
 บ        I want to be in the newspaper, I don't know why, I just do.  I'm    บ
 บ        not sure why my story didn't make it.  Maybe it was because the     บ
 บ        evidence they had on me was so shaky.  And since I got let go, it   บ
 บ        wouldn't look too good for the police if the story was in the       บ
 บ        newspaper, and then have another story in which they had to let me  บ
 บ        go.                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Perhaps you were not in the newspaper because someone else known    บ
 บ        as the Anarchist stole the spotlight earlier this year?             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DEM : Well, I can't blame it wholy on Anarchist, but partially, yes.  If  บ
 บ        he didn't get into kiddie porn, the RCMP never would have come to   บ
 บ        our area code, and everything would be ok.  But, since the RCMP     บ
 บ        didn't have anything to do with my bust, it still would have        บ
 บ        happened, no matter what.  Basically, he didn't fuck me up, but he  บ
 บ        fucked up the scene here (bhwhahahah... 3 people make up the scene  บ
 บ        in my area code, one of which moved out of my area code and is      บ
 บ        interviewing me right now).                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Now that you are back in the scene, what are your future plans?     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DEM : I don't have any permanent plans as of yet, except that I'm going   บ
 บ        to start coding again (PCBoard Programing Language), and I'm going  บ
 บ        to start supplying for a group run by a friend.  I'll be supplying  บ
 บ        coffee and donuts, not warez, that would be ILLEGAL!!! ;)           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Which groups are you going to be supplying and coding for?          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DEM : I will be coding for pUNC (People Under No Control), and I'll be    บ
 บ        supplying for RTN (Revolution).                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : I noticed you were a member of ACiDiC, ACiD's (Ansi Creators in     บ
 บ        Demand) BBS modding division, why did you leave a group with such   บ
 บ        reputation for a new group known as pUNC?                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DEM : Well, since I'm going to be too busy with school, I'm only going    บ
 บ        to have time to code for one group.  I am very good friends with    บ
 บ        the leader of pUNC, Luptin, so I decided to stay there.             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : You used to run a group called ANGUiSH, and since you can supply,   บ
 บ        wouldn't you rather just stick with your own group?                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DEM : ANGUiSH was just a BBS modding group, so supplying wouldn't be      บ
 บ        much good there.  Plus, I won't be able to supply forever, and      บ
 บ        there are already too many groups in the scene, so it would surely  บ
 บ        fail in no time.  And since there are so many groups, most of the   บ
 บ        good suppliers and couriers are already in good groups, and would   บ
 บ        not leave them for a no-name group.                                 บ

 บ    Reporter : Dark-Elf                  Interviewee : Zion                 บ
 บ    Subject  : Prestige                  Affiliation : Prestige President   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What do you do in Prestige?                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  PSG : I am the founder, the leader, I run the World Headquartewrs, and I  บ
 บ        supply.                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Does Prestige release games or utilities?                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  PSG : Games of course!                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : How many games would you say you release over the period of one     บ
 บ        week?                                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  PSG : As many as we can.  It varies depending on how many titles come     บ
 บ        out per week.  Since we began, though, we've released 90% of        บ
 บ        everything put out on the market in the past 2 months.              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What does Prestige mean or stand for?                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  PSG : It doesn't really stand for anything.  It's just a name we thought  บ
 บ        up two years ago when we were Amiga only.                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Have you had a lot of trouble with egos with your members?          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  PSG : We have no internal problems with egos.  We are working for a       บ
 บ        similar goal.  Just because a member is colorful in speech doesn't  บ
 บ        really matter to me, unless he is putting others down.  Then,       บ
 บ        there's a problem.  I am not the one to decide whether or not my    บ
 บ        members can brag over our work.  We are all here to have a good     บ
 บ        time; so let's have it!                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Are you happy with your group?  Do you think you've been a          บ
 บ        success?                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  PSG : Yes, I am pleased with what we have achieved so far.                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Is Prestige currently accepting new members?  If so, what           บ
 บ        positions are currently available?                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  PSG : Since Prestige is mostly a BBS group with the next MIXED in we are  บ
 บ        in need of modem couriers.  We aren't in the need for any           บ
 บ        net-based members, though.  I get asked 2-3 times a day from        บ
 บ        someone to join the group.                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : About how many members strong is your group?                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  PSG : We currently have 25 very talented members on our team.             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Tell us your opinions regarding other groups.                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  PSG : I don't really give much thought to other groups.  One thing that   บ
 บ        bothers me about today's groups is that they don't really care      บ
 บ        much for quality.  Groups today are more worried about being the    บ
 บ        FIRST to put something up than doing it right.  It's really bad to  บ
 บ        name groups but Napalm is/was a group that had this attitude.       บ
 บ        This is the reason for us starting Prestige.  We wanted to bring    บ
 บ        quality to the scene.                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Have you had any trouble with other groups trying to down your      บ
 บ        group?                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  PSG : Nah, what others say about us is not relevent.  One thing that      บ
 บ        kinda pissed me off was when Napalm stole our crack from Toshinden  บ
 บ        and spread it worldwide, claiming they beat us.  That wasn't very   บ
 บ        cool.                                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Would you say that Napalm is the worst group on the net?            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  PSG : No, Napalm is far from being the worst group.  I bet you didn't     บ
 บ        know that I was in Napalm right before I started up Prestige PC.    บ
 บ        Actually, it was Napalm that made me want to start Prestige PC.     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : So Napalm is lower than the worst group that ever was?              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  PSG : Nah, Napalm is a good group.  It just needs to take its time on     บ
 บ        releasing.  That way it can be sure that its cracks work.  Only     บ
 บ        problem is that we will beat them.                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : So why did you want to start Prestige?  What gave you the idea to   บ
 บ        make your own group?                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  PSG : Prestige exists for one reason alone, today's groups don't care     บ
 บ        about quality.  I was tired of being part of a scene that didn't    บ
 บ        give a fuck if the games worked or not.  You have got to take note  บ
 บ        that Prestige on the Amiga released 79 titles in 7 months, all      บ
 บ        100% working quality games, and never needed a fix.  This is the    บ
 บ        quality I am trying to bring to the PC scene.                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Do you think Prestige is headed for the top?                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  PSG : We are the top.                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : How long as Prestige been around?                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  PSG : 2 years on the 23rd of this month.                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Yet, I have just noticed Prestige on the market.  What happened?    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  PSG : We decided to become more focused on releasing for the PC.  It      บ
 บ        seems that this focusing has changed our group around making it     บ
 บ        one of the best on the net, but the net is secondary to us.  We     บ
 บ        are still mainly a BBS bound group.                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : So do you think Prestige is the best on the net?  If not, which     บ
 บ        group do you feel is?                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  PSG : Yes, I think Prestige is the best on the net.                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Has running a group really taken your whole life away from you?     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  PSG : Nope, not at all.  You just have to know how to delegate            บ
 บ        responsibilities!                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : This is kind of personal but do you have a girlfriend?              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  PSG : I have a wife and kids.  Still, I manage to keep my hours split.    บ
 บ        I have a 24-hour connection to the net so I'm on IRC very often.    บ
 บ        And I manage to keep adequate time to spend with my family, my      บ
 บ        group, and my job.  I run a computer sales and marketing business.  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : So why are you more of a BBSer than an Interneter?                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  PSG : The Internet is good, but it all started on BBSes!  I guess I am    บ
 บ        an old-timer. I think it's better to beat Razor 1911 on Beyond      บ
 บ        Akira or their WHQ than it is to beat them on LA or BBX.  So we     บ
 บ        try to beat them on both.  So far we are beating everyone on BBSs   บ
 บ        and on the Internet with time to spare.  You see, it's really nice  บ
 บ        when you can upload all your titles to your BBS and then to the     บ
 บ        WHQ's of other groups and still have time to win on the net too.    บ
 บ        See my point of quality before speed??  I have been in the scene    บ
 บ        since 1987, in Commodore 64, Amiga, and the PC.                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : So in your time in the scene, has anyone ever really upset you?     บ
 บ        If so, please give me their nicks.                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  PSG : Samir and Mok!  They were in Prestige Amiga.  The organizer and     บ
 บ        the best cracker in the world, hands down.  He retired at the       บ
 บ        prime of Prestige.  We went on an 8-month dry spell and then        บ
 บ        decided to start up the PC division.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Reporter : Rebel Chicken             Interviewee : Druggy               บ
 บ    Subject  : Druggy the Narq           Affiliation : ex-Motiv8 Council    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : There are many rumors spread by Motiv8 members that you are a       บ
 บ        narq.  You've been accused of narqing on many sites such as Nihil   บ
 บ        and Dropship, and you have also been accused of narqing on many     บ
 บ        people in the scene such as Pseduo, Storm, and Sub.  Assuming that  บ
 บ        you do not believe that these rumors are true, then what do you     บ
 บ        have to show to prove that these accusations are not true?          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DRG : I would like to remedy myself from all these rumors that are being  บ
 บ        spread by Motiv8 members.  As far as I know, the site Nihil has     บ
 บ        merely changed ports and has not been busted.  I don't know much    บ
 บ        about Dropship, but it was never on my list, and I don't even know  บ
 บ        the site's IP.  Pseudo has left Motiv8 for another courier group    บ
 บ        called Stealth, therefore his site has not been busted as people    บ
 บ        so stubbornly say.  Storm, whom I have recently spoken to, still    บ
 บ        operates his site with full force, so how can Motiv8 say I busted   บ
 บ        him?  From what I heard, Sub has merely left Motiv8 to be a siteop  บ
 บ        in another courier group called Rapier.                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : So you're saying that you did not narq on anyone?                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DRG : That is all the sites and siteops in Motiv8 who have been "busted"  บ
 บ        and sites that have been dismantled because of my narqing on them.  บ
 บ        It is sad to see one of the more older and respected groups have    บ
 บ        to lower themselves to such a level, as to bring someone down with  บ
 บ        their slowly dying group.                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : There is also proof that private sites that belonged to SIN         บ
 บ        (Sinful Traders), a group in which you were a leader in, was also   บ
 บ        busted.  Why were the siteops from your group busted?               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DRG : Other SIN sites and their operators may have been busted (only      บ
 บ        getting their access taken away from the sites) but that is my      บ
 บ        business and under my jurisdiction, as they were sites in SIN, and  บ
 บ        SIN was MY GROUP, making this whole conflict between myself and     บ
 บ        Motiv8 defunct.  Motiv8 is trying to turn away from the fact, that  บ
 บ        they are beginning to lose their sites to faster groups such as     บ
 บ        GODS and RiSC.                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : How did the siteops from SIN get busted?                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DRG : The actual ways in which of SIN's siteops got caught had nothing    บ
 บ        to do with me.  Random, the siteop of the SIN WHQ was disbanded     บ
 บ        from being system administrator at his business in Mississipi as    บ
 บ        our group filled up his 3 gigabyte HD, rendering no cache space     บ
 บ        available for the server to use, as it was down for maintanence,    บ
 บ        therefore crashing the system.  The other system administrators     บ
 บ        was there to resolve the problem and find the pirated material.     บ
 บ        Random was then fired from his job instead of being imprisoned as   บ
 บ        he earlier told me.                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What about the fact that this was his Random's second bust?  You    บ
 บ        mentioned in RCN #16 that this was Random's second bust?  Is there  บ
 บ        some discrepancy in your story?                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DRG : The same thing happened before.  His HD got filled.  Ask anyone     บ
 บ        who was in SIN at the time.  He found out when he got to work the   บ
 บ        next day, deleted the pirated software.  The other system           บ
 บ        administrator came, and blamed it on Random, as vital information   บ
 บ        towards the business was to be stored on the site, and Random was   บ
 บ        new there.                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : That answer only covers how Random got busted.  I've also been      บ
 บ        informed that another SIN siteop, Nettwerk, was recently busted.    บ
 บ        How was Nettwerk busted?                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DRG : Nettwerk, a new addition to our crew at SIN, was busted even        บ
 บ        before his site was fully functional.  Therefore his apprehension   บ
 บ        had absolutely no connection to the site list I distributed to my   บ
 บ        group.                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : You have shown that the rumors started by Motiv8 against you might  บ
 บ        just be rumors, but I want to know WHY Motiv8 would do such a       บ
 บ        thing?  What do they have to gain?  It makes no sense that Motiv8   บ
 บ        would start rumors to say taht you are a narq, perhaps they are     บ
 บ        not rumors?                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DRG : Rumors they are, I am not a narq.  I have run and maintained 3 and  บ
 บ        now 4 groups.  The way I narqed was a list I sent off to my SIN     บ
 บ        members a WEEK before joining Motiv8, which would render their      บ
 บ        sayings as bullshit, for some of their siteops were with us.  The   บ
 บ        siteops and my former members can reference this.                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Reporter : Rebel Chicken             Interviewee : EndoKuken            บ
 บ    Subject  : RTN (Revolution)          Affiliation : Revolution Leader    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Many people know that Revolution is a group that specializes in     บ
 บ        foreign software, why does Revolution specialize in releasing only  บ
 บ        foreign software?  Is it because Revolution has no suppliers that   บ
 บ        can release US software?                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RTN : Well, Revolution is indeed a foreign release group and we do        บ
 บ        specialize in Chinese/Japanese games.  The reason I release these   บ
 บ        games is because there are a lot of Chinese/Japanese people in the  บ
 บ        scene that want such games.  Since I'm Chinese, I am also able to   บ
 บ        enjoy quality Chinese/Japanese games.  As for suppliers that can    บ
 บ        release US software, I do have a few of them.                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : I am crazy about a Japanese cartoon show called Sailor Moon, and I  บ
 บ        also heard that there's a Sailor Moon Game and Screen Saver for     บ
 บ        the PC.  If you find either the Sailor Moon Game or the Sailor      บ
 บ        Moon Screen Saver, make sure you release it.  Anyway, if            บ
 บ        Revolution specializes in releasing only Chinese/Japanese           บ
 บ        software, how come I just saw you guys release a US utility?        บ
 บ        Perhaps that was a fake release?                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RTN : No, that was not a fake release.  Revolution does pull off some US  บ
 บ        utilities faster than other groups because Revolution does have US  บ
 บ        suppliers as I mentioned before.  It is definitely not a fake       บ
 บ        release, in fact, it was a $900 utility that I would never pay      บ
 บ        that much for.  As for the Sailor Moon PC Game and Screen Saver, I  บ
 บ        am a big fan myself and recently purchased Sailor Moon Super Stars  บ
 บ        for my Playstation.                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Many people in the scene comment that releasing Chinese/Japanese    บ
 บ        software is lame, and I even know some RiSC (Rise in Superior       บ
 บ        Couriering) BBSes that nuke off foreign Chinese/Japanese software,  บ
 บ        but do not nuke off software that come from other countries such    บ
 บ        as France and Germany.  Why do you feel that is the case?           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RTN : Hahahahaha, you're funny :).                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Thanks, but do answer the question.                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RTN : People can say what they want, it's their personal opinion and I    บ
 บ        respect that.  As for RiSC boards nuking foreign software, I don't  บ
 บ        worry so much about.  The releases still get out and even if        บ
 บ        people didn't get it in time before they SysOps and SiteOps nuke    บ
 บ        it, they can still come to me and ask for the releases.  I'll be    บ
 บ        more than happy to help them with that.                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Have you ever encountered problems in the past where people would   บ
 บ        just come up to you and say that Chinese/Japanese software is       บ
 บ        lame, and that Revolution is lame for releasing them?               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RTN : I've had all these people come into channel #RTN and just start     บ
 บ        bitching at me.  People come up to me telling me how lame I am and  บ
 บ        how lame Revolution is as a whole, but I just tell them to mind     บ
 บ        their own business.  Even though they still keep bugging me,        บ
 บ        there's really nothing I can do about it, and I don't want to       บ
 บ        kick-ban anyone for such a stupid reason.                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Not all Chinese/Japanese games require that you know how to read    บ
 บ        in a foreign language.  There are some action games that could be   บ
 บ        in Hieroglyphics, and the fact that it's in some weird language     บ
 บ        does not effect the game play at all.  When Revolution releases a   บ
 บ        game, is there a way one can tell whether the game is purely        บ
 บ        action, and thus does not require knowledge in a foreign language?  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RTN : That information is given in the NFO of the release, but if the     บ
 บ        release is for DOS/V or WIN/V, then the game is most likely in      บ
 บ        either Chinese or Japanese.  I have yet to come across any          บ
 บ        Chinese/Japanese action games which does not require knowledge of   บ
 บ        a foreign language.  When releasing a game, we do try to keep that  บ
 บ        in mind, and thus, we focus more on RPGs and AVGs.  AVGs are also   บ
 บ        known to most people as Pornos.  I personally like the RPGs, but    บ
 บ        an AVG is nice every once in a while.                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What does DOS/V and WIN/V stand for?                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RTN : DOS/V is DOS with Chinese/Japanese fonts.  WIN/V is a background    บ
 บ        program run in Windows 3.0+ which enables Chinese/Japanese fonts.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Does one need to have DOS/V and WIN/V in order to run a             บ
 บ        Chinese/Japanese game?                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RTN : Not always, most of the games are meant for DOS and will soon be    บ
 บ        optimized for Windows 95.                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : There are only two groups I know of that specialize in              บ
 บ        Chinese/Japanese software, Dragon and Revolution.  Is there         บ
 บ        animosity between the two groups since both groups compete in the   บ
 บ        same type of releases?                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RTN : First of all, there are many more groups that specialize in         บ
 บ        Chinese/Japanese software that have yet to get around on the        บ
 บ        Internet.  I have nothing against Dragon and they have nothing      บ
 บ        against me (I think).  I originally tried joining Dragon but I was  บ
 บ        told they didn't want anymore suppliers.  Members between the two   บ
 บ        groups get along fairly well.  I say that because I don't know      บ
 บ        many Dragon members :).                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Is there a possibility that Revolution will be releasing more and   บ
 บ        more US software in the future?  What do you see happening to       บ
 บ        Revolution in the future?                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RTN : Basically, I just want to share my Chinese/Japanese games with      บ
 บ        other people who can understand and appreciate the anime graphics.  บ
 บ        As for the US releases, I really am not sure, I'd have to talk it   บ
 บ        over with my council, seniors, and suppliers.                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
