 บ    Reporter : Rebel Chicken             Interviewee : The Edge             บ
 บ    Subject  : CoRE                      Affiliation : CoRE Leader          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : How did CoRE start up?  According to my sources, CoRE started out   บ
 บ        when a merge between a few smaller courier groups took place, is    บ
 บ        that true?                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  COR : Actually, CoRE was formed a few weeks ago when the two courier      บ
 บ        groups Total Kaos and Violation decided to merge.  The two groups   บ
 บ        talked it over a bit and thought it would be better to work         บ
 บ        together.                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Why did Total Kaos and Violation decide to merge?  When the did     บ
 บ        the merge take place.  Were all the members of Total Kaos and       บ
 บ        Violation brought into CoRE?  Were there any members that was cut   บ
 บ        during the merging process?                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  COR : Total Kaos and Violation had similar members and similar            บ
 บ        principles.  Stank-E and I agreed that we'd be better off together  บ
 บ        than seperate.  Almost all members from Violation came into CoRE    บ
 บ        except for the President Venom and Senior Wildd.  Venom and I       บ
 บ        still have good relations because we are good friends.  Wildd and   บ
 บ        I get along fine and he is now heading up Sinful Traders.  Some     บ
 บ        members from Total Kaos were cut from the merge because they never  บ
 บ        showed up.  Cuts and things have been made to inactive members and  บ
 บ        it seems we have a real working team now.  I am quite happy.        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Have there been any problems that resulted from the merge?          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  COR : From what I have seen, the merge has been perfect.  We did not      บ
 บ        have fights or anything during the merge because it was all very    บ
 บ        well planned out.                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : It seems to me then that CoRE is a very organized group, I've       บ
 บ        noticed a bunch of people messaging me to go into channel           บ
 บ        #CoREFiles to offer, and they keep bugging me until I /ignore them  บ
 บ        or actually join #CoREFiles.  Why did CoRE start up channel         บ
 บ        #CoREFiles, and why do your members keep bugging so many people to  บ
 บ        offer in there?  I just joined #CoREFiles about 2 minutes ago only  บ
 บ        to find out that there were 2 people idling in there.               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  COR : Thanks for letting me know, I will address this issue with the      บ
 บ        rest of CoRE.  CoRE's internet coordinator, Palm, is in charge of   บ
 บ        the affairs of channel #CoREFiles.  He is with Motiv8 and started   บ
 บ        #CoREFiles.  When he is not in #CoREFiles, the channel does not     บ
 บ        run well.  I feel if he wishes to keep the room up, he needs to     บ
 บ        appoint a crew to work with.  Also, bugging people to join isn't    บ
 บ        right, people will join if they want to.  I will address that       บ
 บ        issue.                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : CoRE's internet coordinator, Palm, is also a member of Motiv8, a    บ
 บ        competitive courier group.  Wouldn't he devote most of his time to  บ
 บ        Motiv8's own offer channel, #M8leech, and not to #CoREFiles?        บ
 บ        Isn't there a conflict of interest?                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  COR : I don't involve myself with his personal devotions.  He works well  บ
 บ        for both groups.  If he feels he can keep up both, then he's        บ
 บ        welcome to be in both.  He is a great member and CoRE is glad to    บ
 บ        have him.  His interests really do not matter, #M8leech is a much   บ
 บ        bigger channel.                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : So I assume that all CoRE members are allowed to be in other        บ
 บ        courier groups?  What happens when a CoRE member gets an untagged   บ
 บ        release, which courier group would he tag it for?                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  COR : CoRE members are allowed to be in other groups as long as they      บ
 บ        fulfill their duties as a CoRE member.  Tagging for our group goes  บ
 บ        as follows, if he gets the file from one of our affiliated release  บ
 บ        groups, I expect the release to be tagged by CoRE.  If both groups  บ
 บ        have the same release from the same affiliated group, this may      บ
 บ        cause a problem.  I figure, I could talk with the other courier     บ
 บ        group about solving that.  I am a pretty nice guy and have good     บ
 บ        ideas, so I think we could work out something.  But hopefully,      บ
 บ        this situation won't happen often.  I see most of my members        บ
 บ        devoting most of their time to CoRE.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What makes CoRE different from other courier groups?  Why would     บ
 บ        someone want to devote their time to CoRE when they could devote    บ
 บ        their time for another group such as GODS or RiSC?  Why would       บ
 บ        someone want to join CoRE?  What makes CoRE stand out from the      บ
 บ        dozens of other courier groups?                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  COR : I hope to think that we are beginning to make a name for            บ
 บ        ourselves.  I know that my members work very hard, and my whole     บ
 บ        council works their asses off.  One thing that makes CoRE           บ
 บ        different is that I am not trying to rival any other group.  This   บ
 บ        sounds like major butt kissing, but both GODS and RiSC are well     บ
 บ        respected groups.  They do the same thing we do and I respect       บ
 บ        that.  We are all in the same boat here and it is pretty stupid to  บ
 บ        be fighting.  CoRE is for people who want to do their share of      บ
 บ        work, talk to some people, have some fun and get stuff done at the  บ
 บ        same time.  This has worked so far, and I would like to emphasize   บ
 บ        that the scene is *NOT* life and working in the scene is *NOT* a    บ
 บ        real job.                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Groups such as RiSC and GODS often provide their members with       บ
 บ        cards and access to fast private FTP sites, is CoRE capable of      บ
 บ        providing such things?  If not, what does it provide for its        บ
 บ        members?                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  COR : We are on quite a few private FTP sites that is able to please the  บ
 บ        needs of CoRE members.  If they want other things, they ask and     บ
 บ        they may receive.                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : When Druggy was kicked out of Violation by the senior members, he   บ
 บ        refused to leave.  Why did he refuse to leave?                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  COR : I don't really know, I wasn't there, I didn't vote or anything.  I  บ
 บ        was there when they kicked him out and the senior members yelled    บ
 บ        at me to vote but I refused.                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Why did the senior members vote him out?  Why did they even bring   บ
 บ        up the issue of kicking him out of the group?                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  COR : They told me that he was too strict.  They called Druggy "The       บ
 บ        Hitler of Warez, Upload or be Killed."  I feel bad for Druggy.  He  บ
 บ        tries and tries hard.  I wish him the best of luck in Cartel.       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

  ฿฿฿ฐ฿฿฿     ฿     ฿                       ฿฿฿
        ฿              i  n  t  e  r  v  i  e  w  s !

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Reporter : Rebel Chicken             Interviewee : Endeavour            บ
 บ    Subject  : COPS Doing Shareware???   Affiliation : COPS Founder         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : I've seen COPS (Couriers of Pirated Software) release both games    บ
 บ        and utils here and there, why has COPS not taken the move to        บ
 บ        specialize in one field of releasing, or has it already done so?    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  END : COPS now specializes in utils only.                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Why have you decided to do so?                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  END : Well, I feel that if a group releases anything that it can get its  บ
 บ        hands on, it's really not a very professional group.  But if you    บ
 บ        release within a certain specialized area, such as utils, then it   บ
 บ        makes the group seem more "professional".  Another advantage of     บ
 บ        only releasing utils is that I will be able to trade games for      บ
 บ        utils with other groups, which would help make for good relations   บ
 บ        with the rest of the scene.                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : So COPS trades it's games with other games groups?  Has COPS        บ
 บ        traded games for utils with other games groups yet?                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  END : Well COPS hasn't exactly traded ANY games yet with any groups, but  บ
 บ        we plan on trading games with other groups in the future if we get  บ
 บ        a hold of some hot game releases.  I plan to trade games for utils  บ
 บ        with groups such as ROR (Release on Rampage) and Napalm.            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Just a few weeks ago, I saw that COPS released Blake Stone :        บ
 บ        Aliens of Gold, the files dated back to 1993, about the same time   บ
 บ        Wolfenstein was first released to the public, why would groups      บ
 บ        such as ROR and Napalm want to trade their utils with games by      บ
 บ        COPS which have a reputation of low quality?  Anyhow, ROR has       บ
 บ        already promised to trade its utils and games strictly with         บ
 บ        Mortality and not with COPS?                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  END : Yes, I remember that release of Blake Stone : Aliens of Gold.       บ
 บ        That was a BAD release and COPS apologizes for that, but we don't   บ
 บ        intend to release anything like that in the future.  It was a bad   บ
 บ        call on my part.  Well, if ROR has already made a decision on       บ
 บ        trading utils for games only with Mortality, then that's fine.  I   บ
 บ        will find another group such as Napalm, and if COPS can't find any  บ
 บ        other groups, then fATE (Fast Action Trade Exchange) will be our    บ
 บ        next candidate.                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Most Napalm suppliers are also in grousp such as DOD (Drink or      บ
 บ        Die) and PWA (Pirates with Attitudes), and thus have to supply for  บ
 บ        those groups, so saying that Napalm will help supply utils for      บ
 บ        COPS is definitely out of the question.  On the note of fATE, why   บ
 บ        would you trade releases with fATE?  fATE is a courier group, is    บ
 บ        it not?                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  END : Like I said, I will find some other groups to trade releases with   บ
 บ        after consulting with my council.  Those just happened to be the 2  บ
 บ        groups that I could name off the top of my head.  fATE is official  บ
 บ        couriers for COPS, and fATE does have a releasing section.          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What are some of COPS best releases in the recent weeks?            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  END : COPS has released great software such as Visual Object COBOL for    บ
 บ        Windows 95/NT Beta 3 and WebManager for Win95 Beta v.1.1.3.         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Why are those releases all beta, would it be that COPS has          บ
 บ        suppliers that work for those companies?                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  END : You can say that.                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : As an editor of RCN, I try to keep an unbiased opinion toward       บ
 บ        groups.  However, wherever I go, it seems to me that there is a     บ
 บ        general consensus among to scene to look upon COPS as a really      บ
 บ        "lame" group.  The scene accuses COPS of releasing nothing but      บ
 บ        dupes and shareware, why do you think that is so?                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  END : Haha, well, as I learned from the latest issue of RCN (and I whole  บ
 บ        heartedly agree), is that if you call someone "lame", that person   บ
 บ        who call people lame is the person that is really lame.  But, to    บ
 บ        tell you the truth, we have only released 1 dupe and we have yet    บ
 บ        to anything that can be considered shareware. I don't know where    บ
 บ        they would get the idea that we release in those two categories,    บ
 บ        because every group has their share of "dupes" but COPS has had     บ
 บ        only 1, and the scene should give us credit on that.                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : So you're saying that COPS has never released any shareware or      บ
 บ        freeware, and that COPS has only duped once in its entire           บ
 บ        existence?                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  END : Yes, COPS has only duped once, and COPS has never released          บ
 บ        shareware or freeware.                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Do you lie often?  Anyway, COPS is very fortunate to have fATE as   บ
 บ        its official couriers, how did you acquire such a good standing     บ
 บ        and respectable courier group to become officials with COPS?        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  END : Well, MALiCE used to be official couriers for COPS, but then        บ
 บ        MALiCE kicked COPS out, but before that happened, Doobie from fATE  บ
 บ        was in close contact with me, and when MALiCE kicked COPS out, I    บ
 บ        jumped on the chance to get fATE in as COPS' official couriers.     บ
 บ        fATE has been doing a lot more than some of the courier groups      บ
 บ        around, especially MALiCE, which I think is DEAD now.               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Why did MALiCE kick COPS out as official couriers?                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  END : The reason MALiCE kicked out COPS was because the council members   บ
 บ        in MALiCE were REALLY poor with their members.  There were fights   บ
 บ        within the group all the time.  I had repeatedly asked them to      บ
 บ        support the COPS FTP sites, they merely ignored me.  I got sick of  บ
 บ        MALiCE and the MALiCE members got sick of the council and left.     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What do you see for the future of COPS?  Do you see it becoming     บ
 บ        one of the strong utils groups in the future?  There's a quote      บ
 บ        found in the COPS NFO, which goes as follows "Keep an eye on us,    บ
 บ        cuz we are coming very strong, VERY strong, and we are ready to     บ
 บ        tear it up and take all."  Do you believe that COPS is indeed       บ
 บ        becoming very strong, VERY strong?                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  END : Yes, I think so.  I think that COPS will become VERY strong.  It    บ
 บ        may take a couple of years, but I think that sooner or later, we    บ
 บ        will be as good as groups such as DOD and PWA.                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Don't you think that aspiring to be as good as DOD and PWA might    บ
 บ        be impossible for a group such as COPS?  After all, most people in  บ
 บ        the scene are very stubborn, and most already have their heart set  บ
 บ        to believing that COPS is very lame and only releases freeware and  บ
 บ        shareware even when that might not be the case.  Perhaps, it would  บ
 บ        be easier for you to just kill COPS, and start a totally new        บ
 บ        group?                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  END : Hehe, like how you did to Legacy?  I doubt it.  Maybe it will be    บ
 บ        impossible, but I am sure that we will have "some" impact on the    บ
 บ        scene.  When people COPS releases in the future, I am sure they     บ
 บ        will come to change their minds.  But then again, you never know    บ
 บ        what will happen in the future.                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Yes, that is true, but history does repeat itself.  Anyway,         บ
 บ        according to my sources, you also ran an e-mag called Horizons,     บ
 บ        what happened to it?                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  END : Yes, we were, but a lot of our Horizon writers weren't committed    บ
 บ        enough and soon, the group died off.  I see no reason to publish    บ
 บ        an e-mag if RCN is in the scene.  I think that you guys are the     บ
 บ        best and that there should be no other e-mag.                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : I must admire your tenacity in running COPS, if I were running      บ
 บ        COPS, I would have killed it off long ago, but you seem to be a     บ
 บ        hard worker, what's your secret?                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  END : COPS may not be the best group around, but we are sure as hell      บ
 บ        trying to contribute whatever we can to the scene.  And even        บ
 บ        though we may not have the "best" people in our group, or "known"   บ
 บ        people, there are a lot of new prospective members out their that   บ
 บ        are willing to commit time and energy into a group, even if that    บ
 บ        group may not be as good as DOD or PWA.  When you come into our     บ
 บ        IRC channel #C.O.P.S., you would hardly recognize anyone there.     บ
 บ        That's because these members are the NEW batch of people coming     บ
 บ        into the scene.                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ    Author  : Tuxedo Mask                                                   บ
 บ    Subject : GODS (Guild of Distributors) Meeting Log                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The following is a logfile of GODS (Guild of Distributors) first      บ
 บ  meeting in channel #Divine.  The following contains material pertaining   บ
 บ  to GODS, and their relationship with other courier groups such as RiSC    บ
 บ  and Damage.  GODS later comes up with the suggestion to steal some of     บ
 บ  RiSC's fastest sites and boards, but will GODS succeed?                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Lester> Ok, let's go.  Quazimodem, speak :)                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <DAVnGOL> Quazimodem, start the meeting.                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Quazimodm> Ahem.  First of all, on behalf of the GODS staff, I want to   บ
 บ              welcome all of you to the revival of the Guild of             บ
 บ              Distributors.                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <TClaw> Oh yeah, before we start, who is logging?                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Quazimodm> It is hard to believe that after being away from the scene    บ
 บ              from what seems like ages, and after popping in my head       บ
 บ              every once in a while to see how the scene is doing, I'd see  บ
 บ              how things have changed.  I type fast don't I?  I see some    บ
 บ              new, and some old and familiar faces.  It's comforting to be  บ
 บ              acknowledged after putting a lot of effort and sacrifice      บ
 บ              (phonebills, phreaking, etc.) into the scene a couple years   บ
 บ              ago.  Anyway, a bit of history, I was not one of the          บ
 บ              "founders" of GODS (at least technically I'm not).  I was     บ
 บ              running Quantum Traders.  I was approached by the leaders of  บ
 บ              a number of couriering groups at the time looking to merge.   บ
 บ              It wasn't until I had a "meeting" with Slice&Dice where I     บ
 บ              found out that a lot of how the two of us ran things were a   บ
 บ              bit of the same.  Quantum Traders merged with GODS in 1994    บ
 บ              and became of one of best and most recognized couriering      บ
 บ              groups in the scene!  One of the things I want to clarify     บ
 บ              here is the "foundation" and philosophy of GODS.  The         บ
 บ              leaders, Slice&Dice and I, believed in what all couriering    บ
 บ              groups believe and strive for, and that's being the fastest   บ
 บ              in trading warez to all the boards, sites, etc.  Our goal     บ
 บ              was to put GODS on the map, that simple.  But we wanted to    บ
 บ              accomplish that by compiling the BEST, "cream of the crop"    บ
 บ              traders and couriers that we could find, because we have      บ
 บ              equaled the need to have QUALITY couriers and SPEED in        บ
 บ              trading.  Last week, one of our old traders who has been      บ
 บ              very active in the scene, David & Goliath, found me on IRC    บ
 บ              and approached me about the revival of GODS.  Having been so  บ
 บ              out of the scene, he had recapped me on the progress which    บ
 บ              he, as well as some others, has taken upon themselves to      บ
 บ              bring back the "Divine Power", the revival of GODS.  I want   บ
 บ              to commend David & Goliath for having the desire and          บ
 บ              persistency to make this all happen.  Finally, before         บ
 บ              handing this over to David & Goliath or Lester, I want you    บ
 บ              all to remember what GODS stood for.  Consider yourselves a   บ
 บ              part of history being in one of the best couriering groups    บ
 บ              in the scene.  No, GODS isn't OMNIPOTENT or OMNIPRESENT,      บ
 บ              yet!  But we will if we all pull together and strive to make  บ
 บ              GODS 1996 rip the fucking scene up!! :)                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <DAVnGOL> Haha.                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Lester> Woo good job :)                                                  บ

 บ            to add to that bro?                                             บ

 บ  <DrmWeaver> I would, but I don't want to put too much of a damper on the  บ
 บ              hype.  But there are certain things we must consider.  And    บ
 บ              no, I don't type as fast as my old bro Quazimodem.  I'm glad  บ
 บ              to have been approached by both Quazimodem and David &        บ
 บ              Goliath to follow up on a group I once belonged to.  I think  บ
 บ              that all I really want to do at this point is to take some    บ
 บ              time and talk to all of you individually later on this week.  บ
 บ              So for now, I think I will let David & Goliath procede.  Hi   บ
 บ              Lester.                                                       บ

 บ  <DrmWeaver> Oh, sorry.  My concerns are not bad.  When I said "put a      บ
 บ              damper" on things, I simply meant that these concerns could   บ

 บ              happenings.                                                   บ

 บ  <S_Mobius> Did the meeting start?                                         บ

 บ  <Lester> Hold up Silent Mobius.                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <DAVnGOL> I think the main thing this group needs to do is to work work   บ
 บ            well together, to stop fighting, and to have a peaceful         บ
 บ            atmosphere.  We are not forming this group to make RiSC, and    บ
 บ            other groups look bad.  We are doing it, to be #1 and that is   บ
 บ            our purpose.  We don't want to fight with RiSC or Everlast, or  บ
 บ            to have competitions, but we do want to go out there and rock   บ
 บ            the scene, i.e., rock the FTP sites and rock the boards.  In    บ
 บ            doing this, we want to make sure, that our own FTP sites and    บ
 บ            boards remain very fast.  It is our job to support them.  We    บ
 บ            have a great council, a great senior staff, and some great      บ
 บ            coordinators.  These are all people who have proved themselves  บ
 บ            in the past.  On paper, we have one of the most dangerous       บ
 บ            teams.  Now, we will just have to put it together, and          บ
 บ            actually show everyone how good we really are.  Some people     บ
 บ            have come to me and Lester saying, "Hey, this senior staff is   บ
 บ            too big, and it will be lame."  Well, what I have learned       บ
 บ            while being in the scene is that you cannot judge a book by     บ
 บ            its cover.  Sure, there have been lame groups with large        บ
 บ            staffs, but there have also been succesfull groups like PWA     บ
 บ            for example.  There are so many leaders/seniors/and staff       บ
 บ            members in PWA, and yet we all work great together most of the  บ
 บ            time.  So I think, that we need to pull our resources           บ
 บ            together, get out there, and kick some ass.  And we should      บ
 บ            guess, we should just do it and not think that people will      บ
 บ            think we are lame.  If we go out there, and upload more than    บ
 บ            anyone else, trust me, we will be anything but lame.  We have   บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Hitex                                                         บ
 บ    Subject : Rebel Chicken, Hitex, and Xenon BUSTED!                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      On the evening of June 13, 1996, Rebel Chicken, Hitex, and Xenon      บ
 บ  were all busted in front of Rebel Chicken's residence.  After attempting  บ
 บ  to execute an event that they had planned for over a week, their scheme   บ
 บ  went terribly wrong, and all hell seemed to have broken loose.            บ
 บ  Moreover, the entire backbone of RCN was now in jeapordy.                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Rebel Chicken was about to graduate.  He had a mere 4 hours of        บ
 บ  school left before he could officially be labeled a freshman in college.  บ
 บ  Girls were no longer on his mind, he had already given up on that.  Now,  บ
 บ  he was merely interested in conducting an event known as "The Senior      บ
 บ  Prank."  A senior prank is a collecting of a few seniors to coordinate    บ
 บ  some sort of destructive activity on the school as a way of thanking the  บ
 บ  administration for the caring and enlightening experience the students    บ
 บ  were put through for 4 years, known as "High School."  The plan was to    บ
 บ  leave Rebel Chicken's house at 3:00 am, walk down the hill to Rebel's     บ
 บ  school, and replace the United States flag with a Communist Russian       บ
 บ  flag.  This task would be performed by Rebel Chicken and his friend,      บ
 บ  whom we'll call "John" while Xenon and Hitex were frantically cementing   บ
 บ  toothpicks into the locks of the school as to inhibit entrance into the   บ
 บ  classrooms the next day.                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The four of us departed, and we were now on a mission.  Our first     บ
 บ  obstacle was now met - there was a 24-hour security guard appointed to    บ
 บ  protect the school.  He spotted us, but we kept walking as to avoid       บ
 บ  contact with him.  We rounded the corner and made our way back into       บ
 บ  Rebel's country club.  We walked around for about 30 minutes, spotting    บ
 บ  the guard every once in a while.  Then, something caught our eyes.  The   บ
 บ  guard appeared to be making a shift switch with another guard.  We        บ
 บ  watched attentively until finally we noticed them assume their old        บ
 บ  positions.  So we were wrong.                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      By now, it was nearing 4:00 am, and we were about to make our second  บ
 บ  attempt at entrance into the school campus.  Just as we cut the corner,   บ
 บ  the lights of a police car shone in our faces.  We looked at the car,     บ
 บ  then at each other, and it seemed that symbiotically, we all thought      บ
 บ  alike, and as quickly as we came, we dashed away, 4 bullets fleeing.      บ
 บ  Through the brush, over the bushes, under the trees, we ran, until        บ
 บ  finally we made our way to the street.  Xenon, Rebel Chicken, and I,      บ
 บ  were all "clean" except for the glue and toothpicks present in the        บ
 บ  pockets of Xenon and myself.  John, however, held the main weapon, the    บ
 บ  communist flag.  It's not every day that one sees a guy running around    บ
 บ  with such a flag in this country, especially not at 4 in the morning, so  บ
 บ  we assumed the police would find this a bit suspicious.  As a result, we  บ
 บ  all, in our scurry, decided that it would be to our benefit to keep the   บ
 บ  cops from finding John.  We made our way to the street and when finally   บ
 บ  in pure visibility to the cops chasing behind us, the two cops            บ
 บ  simultaneously yelled "OFFICER, STOP!"  We knew what we had to do.        บ
 บ  Rebel, Xenon, and I all stopped while John kept running.  This, of        บ
 บ  course, would create a big enough diversion for the policemen so that     บ
 บ  John would manage to get away while we would get interrogated.            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      So we stood there, a threesome, flashlights pointed at our faces,     บ
 บ  and two officers, huffing and puffing from the run, in front of us.       บ
 บ  "So, what was all that about?" questioned an officer.  We paused, waited  บ
 บ  for one of us to expel an answer, as Rebel Chicken heroically stated      บ
 บ  "Um, we're just hangin' out!"  "At 4 in the morning?" continued an        บ
 บ  officer.  "Sure <ehem> Why not?" our Chicken replied.  "Well, do you      บ
 บ  know that guy that got away?"  "Who, that guy? Oh, pshaww, ehem, of       บ
 บ  course we don't!! Hehehehehehe," we all replied.  Unbelieving, the        บ
 บ  officers found nothing to disprove our telling.  We explained that all 3  บ
 บ  of us were just hanging out when we saw a guy with a big stick so we      บ
 บ  curiously decided to chase him.  So the officers took our names down, of  บ
 บ  which we gave them fake ones, and the officers then decided that it       บ
 บ  would be in their best interest to walk us home.                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      So we proceeded up the hill to Rebel's house.  We walked in, and the  บ
 บ  officers requested to speak with Rebel's mom.  Uh oh.  We tried to talk   บ
 บ  our way out of getting her down but the officers persisted.               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      We got her down, and, well, I thought for a moment an atom bomb had   บ
 บ  fallen on our roof.  Let's just say it wasn't a pretty site.              บ
 บ  Ultimately, we ended up being lectured for another hour by a frantic      บ
 บ  mother, but we ended up okay.  What makes me mad, though, is that three   บ
 บ  guys in the scene, who should all know the law fairly well, could not     บ
 บ  figure out that these officers didn't see us commit any crime, and        บ
 บ  surely we could have said "There are no grounds by which you can request  บ
 บ  that I call my mother out of bed at this time."  But we didn't think of   บ
 บ  it, and though it could have saved us much yelling, it was too late.      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      So we got off easy, some of us, such as Dr. Jekyll, are not always    บ
 บ  so lucky.  But if this story should be a statement to any of us, it       บ
 บ  should be one to show us that a cop is a very gullible species, and your  บ
 บ  story is true until proven otherwise.  So just because you might not      บ
 บ  think that three half-sane guys would ever, bare-handedly, chase a guy    บ
 บ  with a big stick, doesn't mean a cop wouldn't believe it.                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ


                         ฐ
    ฿฿        ฐ  ฿     ฿฿฿ฐ                      ฐ฿฿฿
     ฿ ฿  ฿฿฿  ฿฿฿   ฿    ฿  r c n          ฿฿ ฿฿
   ฿ ฐ฿  ฿               ฿   ฿ฐ   ฿
 ฐ ฐฐ ฐ ฿฿ฐ ฐ฿ ฿฿ ฐ  ฿฿฿฿฿฿฿ ฐ  ฿ฐฐฐฐฐฐ ฐฐฐ
        ฿        ฐ฿฿฿฿฿฿   ฿฿       ฿฿        
                              ฐ฿฿฿฿฿    ฿฿ฐ฿฿฿฿
 ฿ฐ฿฿      ฿ฐ      ฿฿฿ฐ฿                                 ฿฿฿
      ฿                   ฿            a r t i c l e s !
                    ฐ฿                 ฐ฿

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Hitex (Interview by Thrasher)                                 บ
 บ    Subject : GODS Couriering                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Early this week a new courier group was introduced into the broad     บ
 บ  spectrum that already existed.  It began a bit low-key, not much was      บ
 บ  said about them, but apparently not much needed to be said, as they have  บ
 บ  already made their way up the ranks.  In under a week, we have a group    บ
 บ  that is competitive for the #1 courier group spot.  So, how did it        บ
 บ  happen?                                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Despite common knowledge, GODS (Guild of Distributors) was around     บ
 บ  about two years ago and was quite a large courier group, posing great     บ
 บ  competition for the legendary RiSC.  Recently, RiSC has faced major       บ
 บ  competition from a group called Everlast, but because Everlast's main     บ
 บ  goal was not to beat RiSC, it isn't making too much of a presence for     บ
 บ  itself.  GODS, however, seems to be approaching this game with a          บ
 บ  different attitude.  Though not set out to kill RiSC, GODS is here to     บ
 บ  pose some major competition for it, once again.  Will it succeed?  Well,  บ
 บ  that question has already been partially answered.                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The initial reformation of GODS just one week ago was a result of     บ
 บ  the Digital (DGT) downfall, and Amnesia (AMN) merging.  The best of the   บ
 บ  best from Digital were recruited into GODS, as well as the Amnesia team,  บ
 บ  and then a few random couriers that have certainly proven themselves in   บ
 บ  the scene.  So to date, GODS is not official couriers for anybody, but    บ
 บ  that has definitely not hindered them from tagging nearly 50% of the      บ
 บ  warez out there.  A recent look at Park Central, the RiSC World           บ
 บ  Headquarters, and Malevolence, the GODS World Headquarters, vividly       บ
 บ  shows the GODS presence in tagging and its omnipresence in the scene.     บ
 บ  So though GODS is not yet officially couriering for anybody, it has more  บ
 บ  than shown us how well it will be able to support the groups it does      บ
 บ  courier for.                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      So you want to contact GODS?  Well GODS is currently an invite only   บ
 บ  group, of course with the exception of those rare couriers that for some  บ
 บ  reason were not invited but have more than enough to get in.  So don't    บ
 บ  bother applying.  However, if you would like to get your name out to      บ
 บ  some of the GODS staff, #GUILD on the IRC network will be the place to    บ
 บ  go.  #GUILD is the GODS public channel where they will conduct every-day  บ
 บ  conversations.  GODS, however, does reserve a private channel in which    บ
 บ  they conduct meetings and really get down to business.  This is just one  บ
 บ  example of the organization that this group proves to contain.  Many      บ
 บ  courier groups were presented to us this year, and most wanted to become  บ
 บ  #1, but the main problem that stopped them from achieving this goal was   บ
 บ  a lack of organization.  So far, this does not appear to be a problem     บ
 บ  for GODS.                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A year ago, my area code was extremely active in the scene, and       บ
 บ  though we lacked any REALLY BIG boards, we had plenty of the small ones   บ
 บ  and all releases made their way over sooner or later (most often later).  บ
 บ  During the year, as with all area codes, the BBSs in the area began to    บ
 บ  quit, and we are now left with no more than 5 boards in the whole area.   บ
 บ  We are, however, blessed to have one board that is being supported by     บ
 บ  GODS in the area.  The Lower Level, with its 8 nodes, has greatly picked  บ
 บ  up activity this week, and it is amazing to see the motivation that this  บ
 บ  group has brought to its members.  Now, The Lower Level could easily be   บ
 บ  compared in speed to many of the much bigger and more well-known boards   บ
 บ  in the world.                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Yet as we know, the challenge is not in beating the other groups on   บ
 บ  your own boards, but rather, beating them on their own boards!  This is   บ
 บ  surely the sign of superiority.  RiSC got a total of 652 megs of uploads  บ
 บ  to their WHQ, Park Central.  However, GODS was close behind with 440      บ
 บ  megs.  200 Megs behind and on their first week.  That's pretty            บ
 บ  impressive!                                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      GODS has definitely shown their might this past week, and I have no   บ
 บ  doubt in my mind that they will continue doing so in the weeks that       บ
 บ  follow.  Whether or not they will beat out RiSC or Everlast in the        บ
 บ  long-term plans is a question we will all have, so we will all be         บ
 บ  waiting to see the top uploaders stats this week and next with new        บ
 บ  excitement.  Good luck, GODS, and eat your Wheaties, you're up with the   บ
 บ  big boys now!!                                                            บ

 บ    Author  : Hitex                                                         บ
 บ    Subject : GODS Civil War                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The following is a log file acquired from GODS about 30 minutes       บ
 บ  before the desired release time of RCN #18.  We got word that something   บ
 บ  was happening in GODS' private channel.  We didn't know what, we didn't   บ
 บ  know why.  All we knew was that apparently some sort of a "brawl similar  บ
 บ  to the LA Riots" is going on in there and that it wasn't looking good.    บ
 บ  Anxiously we awaited as the log file came in.  This could be information  บ
 บ  that drastically changed the life of what could have been the #1          บ
 บ  Couriering group around.  So, read for yourself.                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ

 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      As you can see, this isn't good.  This is definitely not going to be  บ
 บ  referred to as good news to any of the GODS members.  However, it might   บ
 บ  make them rethink their admission into the group.  Throughout this messy  บ
 บ  and confused conversation, we see many egos fly, and for future           บ
 บ  reference, this could possibly be what will be looked at as what happens  บ
 บ  when you go from new to #1 in one week.  Was this inevitable?  Was it     บ
 บ  the fate of GODS (no pun intended) before it ever started?  And, of       บ
 บ  course, the most burning question on everybody's mind is, how will this   บ
 บ  affect GODS in the future?  Has it totally corrupted the group, or will   บ
 บ  its leadership be able to survive it? It's hard to say.  We just          บ
 บ  witnessed the departure of a senior member and a member from the group.   บ
 บ  Erupt quickly left right at the beginning of the incident, perhaps this   บ
 บ  flame within him was already lit earlier in the week and this was just    บ
 บ  the kicker?  Slain, "Just a trader," left, but could this be an           บ
 บ  indication to the future of the rest of the traders in the group?  Only   บ
 บ  time will tell, but fear not, RCN will be covering the story as it        บ
 บ  unwinds.                                                                  บ

 บ    Author  : Hitex (Meeting Log by Lucifers Fear)                          บ
 บ    Subject : Tom James Reveals Charges to Students???                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A little background reference.  Greg refers to Demaxxus.  John is     บ
 บ  Carnage, and Lucifers Fear is Nick.  Tom James is an RCMP (Royal          บ
 บ  Canadian Mounted Police - The Canadian equivalent of the FBI) officer     บ
 บ  who busted Demaxxus later to release him on the basis of a lack of        บ
 บ  evidence.  This is a log, supplied by Lucifers Fear, of a chat between    บ
 บ  Carnage and himself.  They all live around each other, and, well, these   บ
 บ  seem to be some of the smartest and bravest guys I've seen.  They know    บ
 บ  the law.  They know it well.  The RCMP is going to have to be a lot       บ
 บ  smarter than they have been to even get CLOSE to touching these guys,     บ
 บ  and, well, with a name like ROYAL CANADIAN MOUNTED POLICE, I'm not too    บ
 บ  sure they'll be able to.                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Tuxedo Mask                                                   บ
 บ    Subject : Syncronys Softcorp Pulling a Napalm?                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Memory prices have finally started dropping, and it's about time.     บ
 บ  While other PC components have gotten cheaper eacy year, RAM prices have  บ
 บ  simply bounced around between $30 and $50 per megabytes for a few years   บ
 บ  now, sometimes even going higher when demand for the chips was            บ
 บ  particularly strong.  How does this effect the people in the scene?       บ
 บ  More and more games and utils released in the past few months require a   บ
 บ  computer with at least 16 megabytes of RAM.  As computer technology       บ
 บ  progresses, the RAM requirements for software should increase as well.    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Part of the deal is that RAM chips use exotic technologies, and       บ
 บ  manufacturers have to make huge quantities of a design to turn a profit,  บ
 บ  so the six or seven major producers in the world haven't had to worry     บ
 บ  much about competition from price-slashing upstarts.  Most RAM chips are  บ
 บ  also made by non-U.S. companies operating outside of the reach American   บ
 บ  antitrust laws, and thus, help lower prices of RAM chips.                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      And so the baseline spec for RAM keeps climbing, from 2 to 4 to 8     บ
 บ  megabytes over the past few years, and now 16 megabytes seems meremly     บ
 บ  adequate for a new PC.  It would be nice if we could trick programs into  บ
 บ  thinking that our PCs had more RAM available, and that's the basic idea   บ
 บ  behind virtual memory, a technique for swapping data that isn't needed    บ
 บ  right away into a temporary file on the hard disk.  Virtual memory has    บ
 บ  been part of Microsoft Windows version 3.0, and the system has always     บ
 บ  worked well enough, though naturally it only works for programs running   บ
 บ  under Windows.                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The biggest drawback to virtual memory is its speed.  Lots of         บ
 บ  swapping slows a PC to a crawl, since hard disk drives are hundreds of    บ
 บ  times slower than RAM.  Utilities like Connectix Corporation's RAM        บ
 บ  Doubler, Quarterdeck's MagnaRAM, and Syncronys Softcorp's SoftRAM use a   บ
 บ  different approach to expand RAM without the speed penalty of virtual     บ
 บ  memory, by using data compression.  The idea of data compression should   บ
 บ  be familiar by now, since it's behind about a dozen other technologies,   บ
 บ  including full-motion video, modems, and file compression utilities like  บ
 บ  PKZIP.  RAM compression utilities claim to fit more data in memory by     บ
 บ  compression program instructions and data whenever they aren't actually   บ
 บ  being used.                                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      They all work within Windows memory management system, so again none  บ
 บ  of these programs will help MS-DOS games.  That could be a great problem  บ
 บ  since most of games released are still optimized for MS-DOS.  And none    บ
 บ  of them is really a substitute for more actual RAM chips, but they can    บ
 บ  produce real-world improvements in some circumstances - all of them       บ
 บ  except one, it seems.  Experienced crackers whom I'm affiliated with      บ
 บ  have disassembled the code in SoftRAM and claim that the utility          บ
 บ  couldn't work as advertised; that there's nothing in SoftRAM that even    บ
 บ  vaguely resembles data compression code.                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Syncronys Softcorp has fooled the market and the scene by selling     บ
 บ  possibly millions of copies of a program that doesn't even work.  It's    บ
 บ  one thing to see Napalm release a game that doesn't work, or to see DOD   บ
 บ  release a util without a serial number, but it's totally outrageous to    บ
 บ  see a company release a $99 program that doesn't do anything.  To say     บ
 บ  that it doesn't work and couldn't possibly work is a serious accusation,  บ
 บ  and being suspicious by nature, I tried a simple test.  After installing  บ
 บ  SoftRAM (courtesy of PWA) on my laptop PC, an older 386 with 4megabytes   บ
 บ  of RAM, Windows initially reported that I had an extra 4megabytes of      บ
 บ  space available.  But when I tried to repeatedly paste a 20,000-line      บ
 บ  chunk of text file that I was editing, I actually ran out of memory       บ
 บ  sooner with SoftRAM running than without.  Since compression programs     บ
 บ  like PIKZIP can shrink text to less than a third of its original size,    บ
 บ  SoftRAM should have really shown its colors in this test, but I saw no    บ
 บ  signs that it worked at all.                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      But here's the part of the story that I find most amazing, I called   บ
 บ  Syncronys to inform them of my little test, and they told me that a       บ
 บ  research conducted by Dataquest found that 82% of SoftRAM users           บ
 บ  experienced increase in computer speed.  I hung up and I concluded that   บ
 บ  SoftRAM is nothing more than "placebo software," and that seems fitting   บ
 บ  enough for a program that reports itself to be working while not          บ
 บ  actually doing anything.  If nothing else, placebo software would be a    บ
 บ  good justification of why piraters should not buy software.               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      You might recall that disk compression utilities like Stacker and     บ
 บ  DoubleSpace were very popular 3 or 4 years ago.  But hard disk prices     บ
 บ  have fallen through the floor and those utilities are just niche          บ
 บ  products now, stopgaps that you might want to download or buy until your  บ
 บ  next new system upgrade or disk upgrade.  With the way that RAM prices    บ
 บ  are dropping, RAM doubling software could meet the same fate as disk      บ
 บ  compressors.  There's really no substitute for actual physical memory,    บ
 บ  and if RAM prices are low enough, there's no good reason to settle for a  บ
 บ  crappy download, and there's definitely no reason to shell out $99 for    บ
 บ  placebo software.                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Dark-Elf                                                      บ
 บ    Subject : Broken Releases By...                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      On June 7, 1996, I downloaded a Prestige release called Big Hurt      บ
 บ  Baseball.  I downloaded all 36 disks.  The first file and the ninth file  บ
 บ  ended up having corrupted ZIPs.  So I went to another site and            บ
 บ  redownloaded the two disks.  So the first file was now fixed, but the     บ
 บ  ninth was still damaged.  Finally, I went to yet another site, and        บ
 บ  ultimately all files worked.  I decided to try and run the game.          บ
 บ  Quickly, I found that the pitcher would never pitch.  It was as if the    บ
 บ  computer player was brain-dead.  So after all the time I spent on         บ
 บ  acquiring the game, it was worthless.  I read the PSG.NFO.  The person    บ
 บ  who released it said he did the release in a rush.  He was going on       บ
 บ  vacation and just released it.  I was on an FTP site and noticed a crack  บ
 บ  released by Prestige.  I decided to download the crack.  I ran it, and    บ
 บ  the pitcher still didn't work.                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      It's little things like this that hurt the scene.  A lot of people    บ
 บ  are not as good with computers as me.  It would have probably taken the   บ
 บ  far longer than it took me to figure out that it was a broken release.    บ
 บ  It is thus of extreme importance that every group test its releases       บ
 บ  before releasing them.  A lot of the stuff that is going around is junk.  บ
 บ  It doesn't work.  Why should couriers have to spend valuable time         บ
 บ  couriering software that doesn't even work?  People often complain to     บ
 บ  the couriers saying they should test the software before they upload it   บ
 บ  to a major board, but we must look at it from their perspective as well.  บ
 บ  Couriers want to get on the top uploader lists, but if they have to       บ
 บ  censor what they can upload, it is inevitable that their competition      บ
 บ  will just upload the file instead, and they will lose out.  What CAN be   บ
 บ  blamed on the couriers is the broken ZIP files.  A courier has the        บ
 บ  responsibility of transfering the files he gets in the exact form that    บ
 บ  he gets them, and it is always his responsibility to test all the         บ
 บ  archives he gets to make sure that all the transfers came through         บ
 บ  properly.                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A while ago Napalm released a game by the name of A10-Tank Killer.    บ
 บ  I downloaded it, and, interested in actually playing it, I joined         บ
 บ  #Napalm requesting keyboard controls for it, as they were not included    บ
 บ  in the packaging of the game.  I also announced to them that I was        บ
 บ  interested in supplying for their group.  They agreed and warned me that  บ
 บ  I have to supply at least one release per month.  I agreed on the         บ
 บ  condition that they give me a text file containing the keyboard controls  บ
 บ  to their release.  The game was one about a bomber plane, and I didn't    บ
 บ  know how to drop the bombs.  We conversed for a while, and ultimately     บ
 บ  after much rudeness on their part, they came to the conclusion that I     บ
 บ  was not going to get the text file because I put a condition on it that   บ
 บ  I would only supply if they gave it to me.  I soon found myself           บ
 บ  kick-banned.  This is something I always disliked about Napalm, but I     บ
 บ  wonder why they would dislike me for it.  It seems sometimes that to get  บ
 บ  a Napalm release to fully work, even if it was properly cracked, you      บ
 บ  actually have to buy the game!                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I ended up contacting Sierra, they informed me that to drop bombs,    บ
 บ  you press enter when you have a target in sight.  As far as Prestige      บ
 บ  goes, I would like to congratulate them, as that is their only release    บ
 บ  that didn't pitch.  These are all the cold facts of the scene today.      บ
 บ  Groups need to pay more attention to what they do, be it courier          บ
 บ  properly, or release completely.  A courier needs to take responsibility  บ
 บ  for his job and his job only, but a releaser needs to make sure that the  บ
 บ  end user gets not only a properly working game, but one that he will      บ
 บ  know how to use.                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

    ฿฿        ฐ  ฿     ฿฿฿ฐ                      ฐ฿฿฿
     ฿ ฿  ฿฿฿  ฿฿฿   ฿    ฿  r c n          ฿฿ ฿฿
   ฿ ฐ฿  ฿               ฿   ฿ฐ   ฿
 ฐ ฐฐ ฐ ฿฿ฐ ฐ฿ ฿฿ ฐ  ฿฿฿฿฿฿฿ ฐ  ฿ฐฐฐฐฐฐ ฐฐฐ
        ฿        ฐ฿฿฿฿฿฿   ฿฿       ฿฿        
                              ฐ฿฿฿฿฿    ฿฿ฐ฿฿฿฿

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Dark-Elf                                                      บ
 บ    Subject : Choosing a Nickname                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Join any IRC channel today and you're bound to find some of the       บ
 บ  weirdest nicknames around.  Let's take RCN for an example.  Today, I      บ
 บ  joined #RCN and saw the following striking names : Endokuken, Spy of      บ
 บ  Quartex, Rebel Chicken, and a few more.  Endokuken?  Now tell me, where   บ
 บ  in the hell does a guy come up with a name like that?  Maybe it means     บ
 บ  something in another language that I'm not familiar with, but it seems    บ
 บ  pretty random to me.  Is that bad?  Of course not!  In fact, Endokuken    บ
 บ  is Hitex's favorite nickname.  Whenever he sees the guy around, he can't  บ
 บ  help but yell "ENDOKUKEN ENOKUKEN ENDOKUKEN!!" Spy of Quartex?  Maybe he  บ
 บ  got it out of a movie?  Rebel Chicken?  No comment.                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      So, when you're out choosing a name, for any reason -- maybe you're   บ
 บ  new to the scene, maybe you did something bad and hope that if you        บ
 บ  change your name, nobody will recognize you -- either way, you should     บ
 บ  take the following steps first.                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      1.) Think about your interests.  You don't want to pick the name      บ
 บ          Rebel Chicken if you're a vegetarian, for example.                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      2.) Look through the science book, or any other book that could       บ
 บ          contain weird cool words in it.  The dictionary often works,      บ
 บ          too, but be forewarned, CHECK THE DEFINITION.  Research books     บ
 บ          tend to have words that sound cool but ones that you wouldn't     บ
 บ          exactly want to be represented by.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      3.) Combine words that have to do with your life.  But again, be      บ
 บ          forewarned.  This step majorly depends on who you are and how     บ
 บ          you want to portray yourself.  For example, if our Rebel Chicken  บ
 บ          were to go by this step, he would probably have chosen a name     บ
 บ          like "Never Touched a Girl," but he thought it wiser to portray   บ
 บ          himself as a chicken gone bad.                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I decided to venture out and interview a few people about how and     บ
 บ  why they chose their nicks.  The following are the interviews :           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <RCN> How did you think of your nickname?                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Oxygen> It just sort of popped in my head.  My nick sounds better then   บ
 บ  Hydroboy or Atomman.                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <RCN> What do you mean "popped in your head?"  Do you, by nature,         บ
 บ  constantly think of Oxygen???                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Oxygen> Well, to be honest, I thought of it like this.  A name has to    บ
 บ  mean something.  I was new to the scene and prefered not to have some     บ
 บ  lame nickname.  So I thought of one thing we all can't live without.      บ
 บ  The one thing we all need.  Oxygen!!  No one else would ever think of it  บ
 บ  that way, I knew that, but it's unique, so it works!  By the way, they    บ
 บ  call me "Oxy" for short :-).                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <RCN> How did you think up your nick?                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <RoadRebel> A friend gave it to me 16 years ago.                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <RCN> Why?                                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <RoadRebel> Hmmm no, make it like 12 years ago, it was because of a car   บ
 บ  I drove called a rebel, and people thought it was a road runner, thus     บ
 บ  Road Rebel.                                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <RCN> A car called rebel??                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <RoadRebel> Yes, I had a '67 rebel and my sister had a 68.                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <RCN> What's a rebel car?                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <RoadRebel> It was a car made in the 60's called a rebel, I wish I still  บ
 บ  owned it now.                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <RCN> How did you get your nick?                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <KoKiS> Long story..                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <RCN> Go ahead!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <KoKiS> I'm from a conuntry where cocaine is a "cheap" thing and when I   บ
 บ  moved over to Sweden a friend of mine called me KokainSmuglaren.  His     บ
 บ  girlfriend and I got to be friends and she started to call me KoKiS.  To  บ
 บ  this day, they still call me KokainSmuglaren.  So KoKiS is short for      บ
 บ  that.  There was a thing about it just as I got the nickname.  The        บ
 บ  newspapers had articles about the rise in cocaine abuse and at the same   บ
 บ  time, the rise in warez.                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <RCN> How did you get your nick?                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <DarkSoul> I don't know.  I just made it up.                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <RCN> What made you come up with it?!                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <DarkSoul> I just said, "Hey, DarkSoul sounds cool, so I used it =])!"    บ
 บ  I thought of the name after I named my board (off of something on TV).    บ
 บ  It was called Armageddon BBS.                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <RCN> Sure, but people don't just go walking around thinking DarkSoul     บ
 บ  for no reason!  If they are, they're mentally twisted!                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <DarkSoul> Armageddon, Darksoul, sounded good together!                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <RCN> What do you mean sounded good together?  There must have been       บ
 บ  something that made you think of DarkSoul besides Armageddon.  That has   บ
 บ  nothing to do with DarkSoul!                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <DarkSoul> Don't ask me.                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <RCN> You choosed the nick not me.  Just answer.  Why the hell did you    บ
 บ  pick and how did you pick DarkSouL                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <DarkSoul> I just DID!                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <RCN> Cause it doesn't taste like apples?                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <DarkSoul> I've had this nick (since I started doing bbs shit) for about  บ
 บ  2 years now.  That's all you're getting.                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <RCN> Fine, if you're not going to cooperate then this interview has      บ
 บ  ended.                                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <DarkSoul> What was this interview for????  You never even told me!       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <RCN> I am not supposed to tell you it takes the fun out of it.           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <DarkSoul> Now you know why I'm not answering =).  You want the truth?    บ
 บ  I really don't know how or why I picked this nickname.  It's been 2       บ
 บ  years and I don't remember.  That's the goddamn fuckin' truth!            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <RCN> Fine then!                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I hope this article helped you out in anyway of improving your nicks  บ
 บ  or even just making your nicks in the first place.  Oh, and remember,     บ
 บ  the nicknames portrayed in this article are not necessarily ones that     บ
 บ  will get you far in the scene, and finally, there's more to a person      บ
 บ  behind his name, and a cool name isn't going to cut it if the person      บ
 บ  behind it isn't.                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
