 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Games                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the 5 best games release groups in the scene.    บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The game didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The game was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  game will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ

 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Games                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the 5 best games release groups in the scene.    บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The game didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The game was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  game will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ
 บ  ณ            Dates of Games Reviewed : 05/23/96 -> 05/29/96            ณ  บ
 บ  ภฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤู  บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Games                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the 5 best games release groups in the scene.    บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The game didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The game was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  game will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ
 บ  ณ            Dates of Games Reviewed : 05/30/96 -> 06/05/96            ณ  บ
 บ  ภฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤู  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ

                                         ฿     r e v i e w s !

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Games                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the 5 best games release groups in the scene.    บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The game didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The game was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  game will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ
 บ  ณ            Dates of Games Reviewed : 06/06/96 -> 06/12/96            ณ  บ
 บ  ภฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤู  บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Utils                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the 5 best utils release groups in the scene.    บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The util didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The util was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  util will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ
 บ  ณ            Dates of Utils Reviewed : 05/16/96 -> 05/22/96            ณ  บ

                                         ฿     r e v i e w s !

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Utils                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the 5 best utils release groups in the scene.    บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The util didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The util was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  util will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ
 บ  ณ            Dates of Utils Reviewed : 05/23/96 -> 05/29/96            ณ  บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Utils                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the 5 best utils release groups in the scene.    บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The util didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The util was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  util will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ
 บ  ณ            Dates of Utils Reviewed : 05/30/96 -> 06/05/96            ณ  บ
 บ  ภฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤู  บ

 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Utils                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the 5 best utils release groups in the scene.    บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The util didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The util was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  util will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน

 บ GAME REVIEWS, RATINGS, UN-BIASED OPINIONS, HELP/TIPS FOR INSTALLING GAMES! บ
 บ [][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][] บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  -Rating scale:                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ         (0-19)/100 = In a nutshell, it sucked!                             บ
 บ        (20-39)/100 = Still crap but slightly better.                       บ
 บ        (40-49)/100 = Possibly worth downloading.                           บ
 บ        (50-69)/100 = Pretty decent game. Might want to check it out.       บ
 บ        (70-79)/100 = Worth the download if you like that type.             บ
 บ        (80-89)/100 = Very good, 9 outta 10 its worth the download.         บ
 บ        (90-99)/100 = Excellent game, a MUST download.                      บ
 บ            100/100 = HOLY SHIT I'VE NEVER SEEN A BETTER GAME!              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      RATINGS are based on the game idea, graphics, sound, playability,     บ
 บ  ingenuity, versatility, and a lot of other words ending in `ity'.  These  บ
 บ  games are based on what happens on MY COMPUTER ONLY, unless stated        บ
 บ  otherwise.  I always first follow nfo directions, and if those don't      บ
 บ  work or are not available, I then try other ways.  So just because it     บ
 บ  doesn't work for me, doesn't mean it won't work for you.                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ  +--------\___/๗e๗/aL!\/--------/_____\-----+                              บ
 บ    Back to Baghdad (c) Military Sim. 23/23                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      This game was the biggest bitch ever to install, not because it was   บ
 บ  complic- ated or anything, but because it took fucking forever.  First    บ
 บ  you unarj it, and there's about 1000 small .bmp files which make the arj  บ
 บ  take like around 15 minutes, then you have to edit the .cfg and .bat      บ
 บ  files, and the bat files have like a million lines referring to the dir.  บ
 บ  Then you go to load the game up, and it takes about 10 minutes for it to  บ
 บ  load the terrain and stuff.  And after that it just continues to swirl    บ
 บ  my hd around in circles as it loads and loads.  It just kept loading, I   บ
 บ  went and took a shower, a nap, dinner, etc, while it was loading.  Then   บ
 บ  I came back to find it had stopped loading but had locked up.  I was      บ
 บ  able to see the game <just not play it> from one of the points of         บ
 บ  loading up.  My rating on this game is just a total guess since I was     บ
 บ  not able to play it.  If you even plan to take a shot at this, I'd        บ
 บ  HIGHLY suggest you have at least a pent/133, or you'll wait forever.      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                               RATING : 57/100                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ          There's a 41 disk release, but I'm missing a small piece.         บ

 บ          I downloaded 40 disks and realized there's one I missed....       บ
 บ          DISK 24 WHERE ARE YOU!?!?.                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      But then after searching far and wide, <actually it took about 2      บ
 บ  mins> I was able to find the missing disk 24.  After I spanked #24, I     บ
 บ  unzipped it and well, here's the review:  This is the beta version of     บ
 บ  this MK like game.  The previous release was just a playable preview.     บ
 บ  This one still is a little buggy, but Demolition released a patch to fix  บ
 บ  some things.  It's got a lot of cool things, and the graphics are good.   บ
 บ  But the movement of the characters just has something about it that       บ
 บ  makes you just not like it.  Also you'll need a pent/100+ to play this    บ
 บ  at a decent speed.  Pray for Death isn't going to be the next great       บ
 บ  fighting game, but it might entertain a select few. If you do make the    บ
 บ  effort to get it, might as well get the patch to, it lets you play        บ
 บ  certain modes, and also let's you see the character's stats and stuff,    บ
 บ  even though there is no animation of them.                                บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Welcome to Dear Road Rebel!  This is going to be YOUR column that is  บ
 บ  a cross between Dear Abby and Dave Berry.  The most important part of     บ
 บ  this is YOUR participation.  If you have ever had a question about the    บ
 บ  scene or just a comment, here's the place!  Have you ever wanted to know  บ
 บ  why some people do this or that?  ASK!  I would love to take it to the    บ
 บ  extreme for you and we will be happy to research it!  I hope you have as  บ
 บ  much fun with this as I will!  Remember, this is YOUR column!             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      This week I got shitty letters for Dear RR.  So, instead of           บ
 บ  responding to crap, I will just write my own opinions.  As most of you    บ
 บ  know, I like to share my opinions freely with the whole IRC.  Okay, last  บ
 บ  week's topic was Gays on IRC.  I have seen SOOO many fights about this    บ
 บ  shit in #RCN and other channels that it's become a joke.  It isn't like   บ
 บ  a fag is looking at your ass on IRC, they can't see you, they can't       บ
 บ  touch you, they can't suck you off (although I'm sure some of you         บ
 บ  wouldn't mind).                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      So do some big people get so pissed!?  Could it be that they are      บ
 บ  jealous and just crave a big hairy stinky butt to poke?  Or they are      บ
 บ  actually penis puffers themselves in the closet?  Are they fighting back  บ
 บ  so hard so that people won't think they're gay?  While some of this may   บ
 บ  be true (and picking on the fag channels is fun) the need to argue about  บ
 บ  this in a channel that has nothing to do with it is a joke.  It seems to  บ
 บ  me that the Pillow Biters stay in their own channels, and don't bother    บ
 บ  ANYONE but themselves.  This segregation seems to work nicely.            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I guess the point is, if you don't like them leave them alone.  It's  บ
 บ  a lot like bees, if you don't fuck with them, they won't try to sting     บ
 บ  ya!  And to those that are hiding their feelings behind a guise of        บ
 บ  Machoism and playing the IRC tough guy, well, 2 people came out in the    บ
 บ  last issue of RCN.  I can't name names but, their initials are _GK_ and   บ
 บ  PN, they are free now, and have no problems with their sexuality.         บ
 บ  Hihihihihi!  So that's it for this week!                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  *PS*  GK & PN asked for what you will be seeing next, so enjoy.           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Hetero Rebel              บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Next Week's Topic : How does one know when he is elite?                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      It seems that the scene as a whole is extremely confused about this   บ
 บ  touchy subject, and since we all seem to be so scared of being called a   บ
 บ  "lamer," maybe it would help if we knew what "elite" was supposed to      บ
 บ  mean.  It used to be that the word elite was just a designation for       บ
 บ  warez, such as an "elite board" would be a regular warez board, good or   บ
 บ  not.  So e-mail me and tell me what YOU think elite is.                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ      The following details your forecasts depending on your astrological   บ
 บ  sign.  Each sign designates your personal lucky numbers of the week.      บ
 บ  The following specific areas of focus include those of love and warez :   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Forecast for the week : The pressure is off as Mars transits into fun     บ
 บ  seeking Gemini.  It's not a time to slack, make changes instead.          บ
 บ  Compete in a different realm, try your hand at another art, you may find  บ
 บ  a new calling in the scene.                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Aquarius> (January 20 to Feb 18) : You've found it!  The one warez       บ
 บ             package you've personally wanted for a long time, it may be    บ
 บ             larger than expected but who cares!  Grab a drink, go outside  บ
 บ             and relax while it downloads.                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Pisces> (February 19 to March 20) : You finally finish a task that you   บ
 บ           volunteered for and now can relax, though you were stressed out  บ
 บ           all night and had to get it done in just a few days, it pays     บ
 บ           off, while it may not be the best, you worked hard on it, and    บ
 บ           it will only get better from here on out.                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Aries> (March 21 to April 19) : You have a way of motivating others in   บ
 บ          your group, and those around you.  News comes from a close        บ
 บ          friend that may bring current projects to a halt.  Stick to it,   บ
 บ          and ride it out, you may be able to pull it off.                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Taurus> (April 20 to May 20) : A hated enemy strikes a heavy blow, and   บ
 บ           a self-absorbed leader of yours gets cranky.  While things       บ
 บ           around you look bleak, turn to the ones that matter, your        บ
 บ           friends, while they are not the most popular, they will be       บ
 บ           there for you.                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Gemini> (May 21 to June 21) : An associate pays back a long time favor,  บ
 บ           with an added bonus.  Fight the urge to give up on your          บ
 บ           projects unless you truly feel it is not giving you any          บ
 บ           satisfaction.  The help you have offered a new person leaves     บ
 บ           you with a sense of accomplishment, you have aided someone in    บ
 บ           need, and they will pay you back even if you feel it is not      บ
 บ           needed.                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Cancer> (June 22 to July 22) : An uncommon chat with a person of power   บ
 บ           leaves you with a feeling of respect for him, you have computer  บ
 บ           trouble, OS acting up again, you decide to find a replacement,   บ
 บ           in the form of several files with a stupid code name for them.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Leo> (July 23 to August 22) : A friend nearby is destined to be your     บ
 บ        new partner, and in other areas of interest the ball starts         บ
 บ        rolling, look for new and exciting things to be happening soon,     บ
 บ        and make plans to be there to receive them.                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Virgo> (August 23 to September 22) : Expect a generous offer for your    บ
 บ          skills in the very near future.  Your hard work pays off, and     บ
 บ          you may make it big if you play your cards right.  Look for an    บ
 บ          opening in a position you have wanted for a long time now, and    บ
 บ          go for it.                                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Libra> (September 23 to October 23) : You actually get outdoors this     บ
 บ          week, away from the computer and away from you room.  Enjoy it,   บ
 บ          and when you get back, you'll find your work easier to deal with  บ
 บ          if you take more time to get out more often.                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Scorpio> (October 24 to November 21) : A material sign of prosperity is  บ
 บ            now affordable to you.  You impress the people around you with  บ
 บ            your dedication.  You become deeply involved in how stupid the  บ
 บ            word "cybersex" sounds and vow to blow up any such sites in     บ
 บ            the near future.                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Sagittarius> (November 22 to December 21) : You cheer a friend up by     บ
 บ                inviting him or her to join in a close group of yourself    บ
 บ                and allies, give a second chance to a person you thought    บ
 บ                was lame.  A group effort won't fly without your talent     บ
 บ                and input, so give it your best.                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Capricorn> (December 22 to January 19) : You gain the advantage in an    บ
 บ              important deal and should act quickly, though be cautious it  บ
 บ              may cause your friends to become in danger.  Your modesty     บ
 บ              and hard work is noted and appreciated for once.              บ

 บ  audience of users on the Internet.  They use the most efficient and       บ
 บ  fastest methods possible.                                                 บ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      In an effort to stop software piracy on the Internet, I have been     บ
 บ  monitoring various groups of users on the Internet Relay Chat network.    บ
 บ  This medium of communication has become very popular with "warez"         บ
 บ  pirates who exchange commercial software illegally.  On the IRC network,  บ
 บ  groups of people come together to use sophisticated methods to            บ
 บ  distribute commercial software to literally thousands of users.  With     บ
 บ  such large scale distribution methods, the software industry is losing    บ
 บ  millions of dollars.                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ  participating in illegal activities.  But I can direct you to where       บ
 บ  evidence can be found.  If you are permitted to do so, I suggest that     บ
 บ  you take a brief scan of the user's home-directory and check for any      บ
 บ  suspicious files.  If you cannot do this, I recommend that you keep a     บ
 บ  close eye on this user and watch for any unusual activities.  Please      บ
 บ  take whatever action is appropriate in dealing with these matters as      บ
 บ  stated in your organization's Internet Policy Agreement or Network        บ
 บ  Etiquette Policy.                                                         บ

 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ

 บ  From jeppe Tue Apr  9 14:03:06 1996                                       บ
 บ  Subject: Software Piracy from x@x.x.fi (fwd)                              บ
 บ  To: x (Mr. X)                                                             บ
 บ  Date: Tue, 9 Apr 1996 14:03:05 +0000 (EET DST)                            บ
 บ  X-Mailer: ELM [version 2.4 PL23]                                          บ
 บ  MIME-Version: 1.0                                                         บ
 บ  Content-Type: text/plain; charset=ISO-8859-1                              บ
 บ  Content-Transfer-Encoding: 8bit                                           บ
 บ  Status: RO                                                                บ
 บ  X-Status:                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I have found a user in your Internet domain who plays a large role    บ
 บ  in the distribution of copyrighted software on the Internet.  This user   บ
 บ  uses the nickname "BN" and uses the account "x@x.x.fi.".  He/she is a     บ
 บ  member of an underground group called "Rapier."  This group is dedicated  บ
 บ  to the transfer of illegal commerical software to a large audience of     บ
 บ  users on the Internet.  They use the most efficient and fastest methods   บ
 บ  possible.                                                                 บ
 บ                                        Thanks again,                       บ
 บ                                        Chris Carter                        บ
 บ                                        International Internet Association  บ
 บ                                        chrisc@free.org                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I believe this user, Chris Carter, is violating numerous laws, to     บ
 บ  include guidelines set forth by the Electronic Frontier Foundation        บ
 บ  (EFF).  His means of monitoring are clearly illegal in the United         บ
 บ  States.  He is known to use hacked accounts, send false mail, hide his    บ
 บ  address, monitor channels in "IRC" through stealth modes - his presence   บ
 บ  not visible to users of the channels.  He is also making great            บ
 บ  accusations with no evidence causing undue harassment and libel.  Undue   บ
 บ  conflict between user and administrator and possibly resulting in the     บ
 บ  loss of accounts, if not involvement by state/local/federal authorities.  บ
 บ  Chris Carter's tactics seem to be strategic and premeditative in nature,  บ
 บ  a direct attack on the reputation of whomever he chooses to harass.       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      It is encouraged that the unethical and unlawful behavior of Chris    บ
 บ  Carter be stopped, to protect privacy, freedom of speech, reputations of  บ
 บ  the innocent and prevent him from abusing any other computer systems      บ
 บ  through subversive and/or illegal "hacking" methods.                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Chris Carter certainly gets around.  Upon mention of his name, many   บ
 บ  people have spoken out in outrage at his actions and methods. This        บ
 บ  e-mail is a collective result of concerned citizens in both the United    บ
 บ  States and abroad.  To my knowledge, there are seven other instances of   บ
 บ  such accusations sent via e-mail with no support.                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Upon contact, a system administrator from the first provider has      บ
 บ  stated that they have checked the files of the user in question,          บ
 บ  permissible by a written legal form signed by the account purchaser, and  บ
 บ  have not found a single thing of illegal nature.  Why is this violation   บ
 บ  of privacy necessary due to the likes of Mr. Carter, who does not seem    บ
 บ  to respect the rights of innocent people?  One must wonder whether        บ
 บ  Carter's basis for these accusing messages has anything to do with the    บ
 บ  reason of "software piracy" as Carter states.  If so, his observations    บ
 บ  are error-prone.                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The second provider involved has not commented.                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Thank you for your time and, hopefully, support.  Chris Carter is a   บ
 บ  criminal by any standards and must be dealt with by legal means before    บ
 บ  spreading more harm among the Internet community.                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ  boggling "YOU DON'T KNOW NOTHIN'" questions!  Enter all your answers in,  บ
 บ  and when you feel you're happy with them, press F10 and the computer      บ
 บ  will tally up your score and spit it out at you.  For every question you  บ
 บ  missed, the computer will indicate the correct answer.  Oh, and if you    บ
 บ  feel like "You Don't Know Nothin'" midway through the quiz and don't      บ
 บ  want to embarrass yourself with an incredibly low score, press ESC and    บ
 บ  you'll be back on the bright side of RCN, the awesome music will calm     บ
 บ  you down, and all will be well again.. enjoy!                             บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Hitex                                                         บ
 บ    Subject : Chicken-Watch : Part Trois                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      So I thought last week's Chicken-Watch would be the last.  I had      บ
 บ  finally decided it was truly 100% hopeless this time.  Well, I was        บ
 บ  right.  So I was going through my hard drive last night deleting all the  บ
 บ  crap I didn't need any more when I made my way to the Telemate Edit       บ
 บ  directory.  For those of you that don't know, Telemate is a               บ
 บ  communications program that has a built-in notepad like thing so you can  บ
 บ  jot down notes to yourself while online.  Very useful when you have 30    บ
 บ  people messaging you and you don't know who's who so you write down       บ
 บ  notes in there.  Well I save little things in there, in the Edit          บ
 บ  directory, and once a month I sift through it and delete the crap I       บ
 บ  don't need.                                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      So I was viewing each file separately to make sure I reallly didn't   บ
 บ  need it when I made my way to a "letter.txt."  Out of instinct, I         บ
 บ  assumed it was probably some reader mail regarding RCN, so when I read    บ
 บ  the first few lines :                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      "Okay, I lied, I did kinda write what I said earlier :)  That's       บ
 บ  because I thought (knew) that if I didn't, I'd probably stutter and make  บ
 บ  myself look stupid :(.  Here's what I said (or tried to say) - in Email   บ
 บ  format;"                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I was just a tad confused to say the least.  I decided to read on,    บ
 บ  perhaps the next few lines would reveal a bit more :                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      "When I see you at school, I see a kind and generous person.  You're  บ
 บ  especially pretty when you give one of your pretty smiles :) ..."         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      And that was the kicker.  OH MY FUCKING GOD!!!  Hah, now I            บ
 บ  remembered!  Yes, it was about a month ago, I was at Xenon's house, we    บ
 บ  were working on some coding for RCN, when we got a call from the          บ
 บ  legendary Rebel Chicken.  Of course, I asked him, much like I always did  บ
 บ  at the beginning of a conversation, about the girl situation (or lack     บ
 บ  thereof).  He told me of a new revelation in the story.  Apparently he    บ
 บ  had just gotten Emily's AOL (give her a break, you can't bitch at a girl  บ
 บ  that Rebel likes for having AOL, I don't know why, but you just can't!)   บ
 บ  address and decided to email her.  So I asked him what he said to her,    บ
 บ  and of course, he had the whole thing saved in his saved-messages         บ
 บ  folder.  I told him to read it to me, and I guess he heard some clicking  บ
 บ  in the background so he assumed I was typing what he was saying.          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      He quickly yelled at me to quit typing it, but I said "Wha?  Oh,      บ
 บ  that's not me, it's Xenon coding!!!"  Heh, he bought it.  But of course,  บ
 บ  he reads a little faster than I type, so I told him "Wait!  I'm gonna     บ
 บ  say whatever you say twice so that Xenon can hear it too!"  Heh,          บ
 บ  meanwhile I was frantically typing into my edit window.  When I would     บ
 บ  get too far behind, I would tell him "Hold on, Xenon's mom is talking, I  บ
 บ  can't hear!"  So here, read on.  This is young love in progress!!!        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      "But I haven't seen you smile much lately :(.  I see you here and     บ
 บ  then, but you always seem kinda unhappy :(... Well, I don't know why      บ
 บ  you're sad.. :(, but my guess is that there are people out there who      บ
 บ  don't appreciate you.  That might be true, and if it is, then those       บ
 บ  people who don't appreciate you are just some of the most ignorant        บ
 บ  people around.                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I hope what I say makes sense to you :) may be it'll help make you    บ
 บ  feel better :).  By the way, my email thing snail mails, it might make    บ
 บ  it to your account just a tiny little late :(.  I'll see you tomorrow at  บ
 บ  school :) - AND, be happy :) you're too nice of a person to have to feel  บ
 บ  sad!"                                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      BAAAAAAAHAAHAHAHAH!  Damn, I'll never forget that day.  Check out     บ
 บ  all those :( and :)'s!!!  I guess we know what Rebel Chicken does when    บ
 บ  he's nervous.  Anyway, I don't know about you, but I thought that was a   บ
 บ  pretty sweet letter, and though he makes it totally obvious that he's     บ
 บ  never talked to a girl in his life, it's kind of cute and maybe the       บ
 บ  girls could dig it.  So you ask the outcome of this?  Well, fear not,     บ
 บ  the letter didn't lead to any sort of relationship, read past issues of   บ
 บ  RCN and Chicken-Watch to find out what happened to Rebel and Emily.       บ
 บ  Anyway, I hope you enjoyed this issue of Chicken-Watch, and, though I     บ
 บ  don't THINK there's any more to say, our Chicken always finds SOMETHING   บ
 บ  to make us laugh.                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
